## ğŸ“Š **Power Scale Chi Tiáº¿t**

### **CÃ´ng thá»©c Power Level**
```
Power Level = Base_Power Ã— Realm_Multiplier Ã— Substage_Multiplier Ã— Quality_Multiplier
```

### **CÃ´ng thá»©c Tu Vi**
```
Tu Vi = Power_Level Ã— 1000 (Ä‘Æ¡n vá»‹: nÄƒm tu luyá»‡n)
```

> **âš ï¸ LÆ¯U Ã QUAN TRá»ŒNG Vá»€ IMPLEMENTATION:**
> - **Tu Vi (XP) pháº£i sá»­ dá»¥ng `float64`** Ä‘á»ƒ lÆ°u trá»¯ do giÃ¡ trá»‹ ráº¥t lá»›n
> - **Power Level sá»­ dá»¥ng `int64`** (Ä‘Ã£ Ä‘Æ°á»£c phÃ¢n tÃ­ch Ä‘á»§ kháº£ nÄƒng)
> - **CÃ´ng thá»©c chuyá»ƒn Ä‘á»•i**: `float64(tu_vi) = float64(power_level) * 1000.0`
> - **LÃ½ do**: Tu vi cÃ³ thá»ƒ lÃªn Ä‘áº¿n 39+ nghÃ¬n tá»· nÄƒm, vÆ°á»£t quÃ¡ kháº£ nÄƒng cá»§a `int64`

### **PhÃ¢n TÃ­ch Chi Tiáº¿t Vá» Data Types**

#### **Power Level - `int64` (Äá»§ kháº£ nÄƒng)**
- **GiÃ¡ trá»‹ max**: ~9.22 Ã— 10^18
- **ThÃ¡nh NhÃ¢n max**: ~2 Ã— 10^17
- **Safety margin**: ~99.89% (ráº¥t an toÃ n)

#### **Tu Vi - `float64` (Báº¯t buá»™c)**
- **GiÃ¡ trá»‹ max**: ~1.8 Ã— 10^308
- **ThÃ¡nh NhÃ¢n max**: ~3.9 Ã— 10^16 nÄƒm
- **Safety margin**: ~99.999...% (cá»±c ká»³ an toÃ n)
- **LÃ½ do**: GiÃ¡ trá»‹ quÃ¡ lá»›n cho `int64` (max ~9.22 Ã— 10^18)

#### **CÃ´ng Thá»©c Chuyá»ƒn Äá»•i An ToÃ n**
```go
// Power Level (int64) -> Tu Vi (float64)
func PowerLevelToTuVi(powerLevel int64) float64 {
    return float64(powerLevel) * 1000.0
}

// Tu Vi (float64) -> Power Level (int64) - vá»›i lÃ m trÃ²n
func TuViToPowerLevel(tuVi float64) int64 {
    return int64(tuVi / 1000.0)
}
```

### **VÃ­ Dá»¥ Cá»¥ Thá»ƒ Vá» GiÃ¡ Trá»‹ Tu Vi**

#### **PhÃ m Tráº§n Cáº£nh**
- **Luyá»‡n KhÃ­**: 1,000 - 10,000 nÄƒm (1.0e3 - 1.0e4)
- **TrÃºc CÆ¡**: 10,000 - 100,000 nÄƒm (1.0e4 - 1.0e5)
- **Kim Äan**: 100,000 - 1,000,000 nÄƒm (1.0e5 - 1.0e6)
- **NguyÃªn Anh**: 1,000,000 - 10,000,000 nÄƒm (1.0e6 - 1.0e7)
- **HÃ³a Tháº§n**: 10,000,000 - 100,000,000 nÄƒm (1.0e7 - 1.0e8)
- **Luyá»‡n HÆ°**: 100,000,000 - 1,000,000,000 nÄƒm (1.0e8 - 1.0e9)
- **Há»£p Thá»ƒ**: 1,000,000,000 - 10,000,000,000 nÄƒm (1.0e9 - 1.0e10)
- **Äáº¡i Thá»«a**: 10,000,000,000 - 100,000,000,000 nÄƒm (1.0e10 - 1.0e11)

#### **TiÃªn NhÃ¢n Cáº£nh**
- **Äá»‹a TiÃªn**: 100,000,000,000 - 500,000,000,000 nÄƒm (1.0e11 - 5.0e11)
- **ThiÃªn TiÃªn**: 500,000,000,000 - 2,500,000,000,000 nÄƒm (5.0e11 - 2.5e12)
- **Huyá»n TiÃªn**: 2,500,000,000,000 - 12,500,000,000,000 nÄƒm (2.5e12 - 1.25e13)
- **ThÃ¡i áº¤t TÃ¡n TiÃªn**: 12,500,000,000,000 - 62,500,000,000,000 nÄƒm (1.25e13 - 6.25e13)
- **Kim TiÃªn**: 62,500,000,000,000 - 312,500,000,000,000 nÄƒm (6.25e13 - 3.125e14)
- **Äáº¡i La Kim TiÃªn**: 312,500,000,000,000 - 1,562,500,000,000,000 nÄƒm (3.125e14 - 1.5625e15)
- **Chuáº©n ThÃ¡nh**: 1,562,500,000,000,000 - 7,812,500,000,000,000 nÄƒm (1.5625e15 - 7.8125e15)
- **ThÃ¡nh NhÃ¢n**: 7,812,500,000,000,000 - 39,062,500,000,000,000+ nÄƒm (7.8125e15 - 3.90625e16+)

#### **So SÃ¡nh Vá»›i Giá»›i Háº¡n `int64`**
- **`int64` max**: 9,223,372,036,854,775,807 (~9.22e18)
- **ThÃ¡nh NhÃ¢n max**: 39,062,500,000,000,000+ (~3.91e16)
- **Káº¿t luáº­n**: Tu vi vÆ°á»£t quÃ¡ kháº£ nÄƒng cá»§a `int64`, **báº¯t buá»™c pháº£i dÃ¹ng `float64`**

### **CÃ´ng Thá»©c TÃ­nh ToÃ¡n Äan Äiá»n**

func CalculateDantianCapacity(powerLevel int64, expansionFactor float64) float64 {

// Expansion factors by realm (å¢ƒç•Œæ‰©å±•ç³»æ•°) - Há»‡ sá»‘ má»Ÿ rá»™ng theo cáº£nh giá»›i

    "Qi Refining": 1.0,        // ç‚¼æ°” (Luyá»‡n KhÃ­)
    "Foundation Building": 1.5, // ç­‘åŸº (TrÃºc CÆ¡)
    "Golden Core": 2.0,        // é‡‘ä¸¹ (Kim Äan)
    "Nascent Soul": 3.0,       // å…ƒå©´ (NguyÃªn Anh)
    "Spirit Transformation": 5.0, // åŒ–ç¥ (HÃ³a Tháº§n)
    "Void Refining": 8.0,      // ç‚¼è™š (Luyá»‡n HÆ°)

    "Heaven Immortal": 100.0,  // å¤©ä»™ (ThiÃªn TiÃªn)
    "Mystic Immortal": 200.0,  // ç„ä»™ (Huyá»n TiÃªn)
    "Taiyi Scattered Immortal": 500.0, // å¤ªä¹™æ•£ä»™ (ThÃ¡i áº¤t TÃ¡n TiÃªn)

#### **2. Cáº¥p Äá»™ Äan Äiá»n**
```go
// Calculate dantian level based on cultivation experience (æ ¹æ®ä¿®ç‚¼ç»éªŒè®¡ç®—ä¸¹ç”°ç­‰çº§) - Cáº¥p Ä‘á»™ dá»±a trÃªn tu vi
func CalculateDantianLevel(cultivationExp float64) int64 {
    if cultivationExp < 10000 {
        return 1 // Qi Refining (ç‚¼æ°”) - Luyá»‡n KhÃ­
    } else if cultivationExp < 100000 {
        return 2 // Foundation Building (ç­‘åŸº) - TrÃºc CÆ¡
    } else if cultivationExp < 1000000 {
        return 3 // Golden Core (é‡‘ä¸¹) - Kim Äan
    } else if cultivationExp < 10000000 {
        return 4 // Nascent Soul (å…ƒå©´) - NguyÃªn Anh
    } else if cultivationExp < 100000000 {
        return 5 // Spirit Transformation (åŒ–ç¥) - HÃ³a Tháº§n
    } else if cultivationExp < 1000000000 {
        return 6 // Void Refining (ç‚¼è™š) - Luyá»‡n HÆ°
    } else if cultivationExp < 10000000000 {
        return 7 // Integration (åˆä½“) - Há»£p Thá»ƒ
    } else if cultivationExp < 100000000000 {
        return 8 // Great Ascension (å¤§ä¹˜) - Äáº¡i Thá»«a
    } else if cultivationExp < 500000000000 {
        return 9 // Earth Immortal (åœ°ä»™) - Äá»‹a TiÃªn
    } else if cultivationExp < 2500000000000 {
        return 10 // Heaven Immortal (å¤©ä»™) - ThiÃªn TiÃªn
    } else if cultivationExp < 12500000000000 {
        return 11 // Mystic Immortal (ç„ä»™) - Huyá»n TiÃªn
    } else if cultivationExp < 62500000000000 {
        return 12 // Taiyi Scattered Immortal (å¤ªä¹™æ•£ä»™) - ThÃ¡i áº¤t TÃ¡n TiÃªn
    } else if cultivationExp < 312500000000000 {
        return 13 // Golden Immortal (é‡‘ä»™) - Kim TiÃªn
    } else if cultivationExp < 1562500000000000 {
        return 14 // Great Luo Golden Immortal (å¤§ç½—é‡‘ä»™) - Äáº¡i La Kim TiÃªn
    } else if cultivationExp < 7812500000000000 {
        return 15 // Quasi-Saint (å‡†åœ£) - Chuáº©n ThÃ¡nh
    } else {
        return 16 // Saint (åœ£äºº) - ThÃ¡nh NhÃ¢n
    }
}
```

#### **3. Tiá»ƒu Cáº£nh Giá»›i**
```go
// Determine substage based on cultivation experience and level (æ ¹æ®ä¿®ç‚¼ç»éªŒå’Œç­‰çº§ç¡®å®šå°å¢ƒç•Œ) - XÃ¡c Ä‘á»‹nh tiá»ƒu cáº£nh giá»›i dá»±a trÃªn tu vi vÃ  cáº¥p Ä‘á»™
func DetermineSubstage(cultivationExp float64, dantianLevel int64) string {
    switch dantianLevel {
    case 1: // Qi Refining (ç‚¼æ°”) - Luyá»‡n KhÃ­
        return "Tier 1-10" // ç¬¬1-10å±‚ (Táº§ng 1-10)
    case 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7, 8: // Mortal Realms (å‡¡äººå¢ƒç•Œ) - PhÃ m Tráº§n Cáº£nh
        if cultivationExp < float64(dantianLevel)*10000*0.1 {
            return "Early" // åˆæœŸ (SÆ¡ ká»³)
        } else if cultivationExp < float64(dantianLevel)*10000*0.25 {
            return "Middle" // ä¸­æœŸ (Trung ká»³)
        } else if cultivationExp < float64(dantianLevel)*10000*0.5 {
            return "Late" // åæœŸ (Háº­u ká»³)
        } else {
            return "Perfect" // åœ†æ»¡ (ViÃªn mÃ£n)
        }
    case 9, 10, 11, 12, 13, 14, 15, 16: // Immortal Realms (ä»™äººå¢ƒç•Œ) - TiÃªn NhÃ¢n Cáº£nh
        // More complex logic for 10 tiers (10å±‚çš„æ›´å¤æ‚é€»è¾‘) - Logic phá»©c táº¡p hÆ¡n cho 10 táº§ng
        return DetermineImmortalSubstage(cultivationExp, dantianLevel)
    default:
        return "Unknown" // æœªçŸ¥ (KhÃ´ng xÃ¡c Ä‘á»‹nh)
    }
}
```

## ğŸ§  **Há»‡ Thá»‘ng 3 ThÃ nh Pháº§n ChÃ­nh (Tinh-KhÃ­-Tháº§n)**

Há»‡ thá»‘ng kim Ä‘an Ä‘Æ°á»£c xÃ¢y dá»±ng trÃªn ná»n táº£ng **Tinh-KhÃ­-Tháº§n** (Essence-Qi-Spirit), vá»›i 3 thÃ nh pháº§n chÃ­nh:

1. **Äan Äiá»n (Dantian)** - Trung tÃ¢m lÆ°u trá»¯ vÃ  xá»­ lÃ½ khÃ­
2. **Kinh Máº¡ch (Meridians)** - Há»‡ thá»‘ng váº­n chuyá»ƒn khÃ­ vÃ  tinh
3. **Thá»©c Háº£i (Spirit Sea)** - Trung tÃ¢m Ã½ thá»©c vÃ  tháº§n thá»©c

## âš”ï¸ **Há»‡ Thá»‘ng Äáº¡o vÃ  Ão NghÄ©a (Dao & Profound Meaning System)**

Tá»« **TiÃªn cáº£nh** trá»Ÿ lÃªn, combat vÃ  tu luyá»‡n phá»¥ thuá»™c ráº¥t nhiá»u vÃ o **Äáº¡o** (Dao) vÃ  **Ão NghÄ©a** (Profound Meaning). ÄÃ¢y lÃ  há»‡ thá»‘ng nÃ¢ng cao cho turn-based combat:

### **1. Äáº¡o (Dao) - The Way/Path**

**Äáº¡o** lÃ  con Ä‘Æ°á»ng tu luyá»‡n vÃ  chiáº¿n Ä‘áº¥u, Ä‘á»‹nh hÆ°á»›ng cÃ¡ch sá»­ dá»¥ng nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng vÃ  ká»¹ thuáº­t:

#### **CÃ¡c Loáº¡i Äáº¡o ChÃ­nh:**
- **Kiáº¿m Äáº¡o (Sword Dao)** - Con Ä‘Æ°á»ng kiáº¿m thuáº­t
- **Äao Äáº¡o (Blade Dao)** - Con Ä‘Æ°á»ng Ä‘ao thuáº­t  
- **Quyá»n Äáº¡o (Fist Dao)** - Con Ä‘Æ°á»ng quyá»n phÃ¡p

- **TÃ¢m Äáº¡o (Heart Dao)** - Con Ä‘Æ°á»ng tÃ¢m cáº£nh
- **ThiÃªn Äáº¡o (Heaven Dao)** - Con Ä‘Æ°á»ng thiÃªn Ä‘áº¡o
- **Äá»‹a Äáº¡o (Earth Dao)** - Con Ä‘Æ°á»ng Ä‘á»‹a Ä‘áº¡o
- **NhÃ¢n Äáº¡o (Human Dao)** - Con Ä‘Æ°á»ng nhÃ¢n Ä‘áº¡o

#### **Cáº¥p Äá»™ Äáº¡o:**
1. **SÆ¡ Ngá»™ (Initial Comprehension)** - 1-3 táº§ng
2. **Tiá»ƒu ThÃ nh (Minor Achievement)** - 4-6 táº§ng

### **2. Ão NghÄ©a (Profound Meaning) - Deep Understanding**

- **Quyá»n Ã (Fist Intent)** - Ã niá»‡m quyá»n phÃ¡p

    // Basic understanding (åŸºç¡€ç†è§£) - Hiá»ƒu biáº¿t cÆ¡ báº£n
    BasicUnderstanding float64 `json:"basic_understanding"` // Basic understanding (åŸºç¡€ç†è§£) - Hiá»ƒu biáº¿t cÆ¡ báº£n
    IntermediateUnderstanding float64 `json:"intermediate_understanding"` // Intermediate understanding (ä¸­çº§ç†è§£) - Hiá»ƒu biáº¿t trung cáº¥p
    AdvancedUnderstanding float64 `json:"advanced_understanding"` // Advanced understanding (é«˜çº§ç†è§£) - Hiá»ƒu biáº¿t nÃ¢ng cao
    
    // Profound understanding (æ·±åˆ»ç†è§£) - Hiá»ƒu biáº¿t sÃ¢u sáº¯c
    ProfoundInsight    float64 `json:"profound_insight"`    // Profound insight (æ·±åˆ»æ´å¯Ÿ) - Sá»± tháº¥u hiá»ƒu sÃ¢u sáº¯c
    TranscendentWisdom float64 `json:"transcendent_wisdom"` // Transcendent wisdom (è¶…è„±æ™ºæ…§) - TrÃ­ tuá»‡ siÃªu thoÃ¡t
    MeaningEssence     float64 `json:"meaning_essence"`     // Profound Meaning essence (å¥¥ä¹‰æœ¬è´¨) - Báº£n cháº¥t Ão NghÄ©a
}

// Profound Ability (å¥¥ä¹‰èƒ½åŠ›) - Kháº£ nÄƒng Ão NghÄ©a
type ProfoundAbility struct {
    // Basic info (åŸºæœ¬ä¿¡æ¯) - ThÃ´ng tin cÆ¡ báº£n
    AbilityName    string  `json:"ability_name"`    // Ability name (èƒ½åŠ›åç§°) - TÃªn kháº£ nÄƒng
    AbilityType    string  `json:"ability_type"`    // Ability type (èƒ½åŠ›ç±»å‹) - Loáº¡i kháº£ nÄƒng
    AbilityLevel   int     `json:"ability_level"`   // Ability level (èƒ½åŠ›ç­‰çº§) - Cáº¥p Ä‘á»™ kháº£ nÄƒng
    AbilityPower   float64 `json:"ability_power"`   // Ability power (èƒ½åŠ›å¨åŠ›) - Sá»©c máº¡nh kháº£ nÄƒng
    
    // Advanced properties (é«˜çº§å±æ€§) - Thuá»™c tÃ­nh nÃ¢ng cao
    AbilityCost    float64 `json:"ability_cost"`    // Ability cost (èƒ½åŠ›æ¶ˆè€—) - Chi phÃ­ kháº£ nÄƒng
    AbilityCooldown float64 `json:"ability_cooldown"` // Ability cooldown (èƒ½åŠ›å†·å´) - Thá»i gian há»“i chiÃªu
    AbilityRange   float64 `json:"ability_range"`   // Ability range (èƒ½åŠ›èŒƒå›´) - Pháº¡m vi kháº£ nÄƒng
    AbilityAccuracy float64 `json:"ability_accuracy"` // Ability accuracy (èƒ½åŠ›ç²¾åº¦) - Äá»™ chÃ­nh xÃ¡c kháº£ nÄƒng
}

// Profound Resonance (å¥¥ä¹‰å…±æŒ¯) - Cá»™ng hÆ°á»Ÿng Ão NghÄ©a
type ProfoundResonance struct {
    // Resonance matrix (å…±æŒ¯çŸ©é˜µ) - Ma tráº­n cá»™ng hÆ°á»Ÿng
    ResonanceMatrix map[string]map[string]float64 `json:"resonance_matrix"`
    
    // Resonance effects (å…±æŒ¯æ•ˆæœ) - Hiá»‡u á»©ng cá»™ng hÆ°á»Ÿng
    ResonanceEffects map[string]float64 `json:"resonance_effects"`
    
    // Overwhelm effects (å‹å€’æ•ˆæœ) - Hiá»‡u á»©ng Ã¡p Ä‘áº£o
    OverwhelmEffects map[string]float64 `json:"overwhelm_effects"`
}

#### **D. CÃ´ng Thá»©c TÃ­nh ToÃ¡n Äáº¡o vÃ  Ão NghÄ©a:**

```go
// Calculate Dao stats (è®¡ç®—é“å±æ€§) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n cÃ¡c stats cá»§a Äáº¡o
func CalculateDaoStats(daoSystem DaoSystem) map[string]float64 {
    stats := make(map[string]float64)
    
    // Get primary Dao (è·å–ä¸»é“) - Láº¥y Äáº¡o chÃ­nh
    primaryDao, exists := daoSystem.DaoPaths[daoSystem.PrimaryDaoType]
    if !exists {
        return stats // Return empty if no primary Dao (å¦‚æœæ²¡æœ‰ä¸»é“åˆ™è¿”å›ç©º) - Náº¿u khÃ´ng cÃ³ Äáº¡o chÃ­nh thÃ¬ tráº£ vá» rá»—ng
    }
    
    // Core Dao stats (æ ¸å¿ƒé“å±æ€§) - Stats cá»‘t lÃµi Äáº¡o
    stats["dao_level"] = float64(primaryDao.DaoLevel)
    stats["dao_experience"] = primaryDao.DaoExperience
    stats["dao_mastery"] = primaryDao.DaoMastery
    stats["dao_insight"] = primaryDao.DaoInsight
    stats["dao_wisdom"] = primaryDao.DaoWisdom
    
    // Advanced Dao stats (é«˜çº§é“å±æ€§) - Stats nÃ¢ng cao Äáº¡o
    stats["dao_harmony"] = primaryDao.DaoHarmony
    stats["dao_transcendence"] = primaryDao.DaoTranscendence
    
    // Calculate total stats across all active Daos (è®¡ç®—æ‰€æœ‰æ¿€æ´»é“çš„æ€»å±æ€§) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n tá»•ng stats tá»« táº¥t cáº£ Äáº¡o Ä‘ang hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng
    totalLevel := 0.0
    totalExperience := 0.0
    totalMastery := 0.0
    activeDaoCount := 0
    
    for _, dao := range daoSystem.DaoPaths {
        if dao.IsActive {
            totalLevel += float64(dao.DaoLevel)
            totalExperience += dao.DaoExperience
            totalMastery += dao.DaoMastery
            activeDaoCount++
        }
    }
    
    // Average stats across active Daos (æ¿€æ´»é“çš„å¹³å‡å±æ€§) - Stats trung bÃ¬nh cá»§a cÃ¡c Äáº¡o Ä‘ang hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng
    if activeDaoCount > 0 {
        stats["total_dao_level"] = totalLevel
        stats["total_dao_experience"] = totalExperience
        stats["total_dao_mastery"] = totalMastery
        stats["active_dao_count"] = float64(activeDaoCount)
        stats["average_dao_level"] = totalLevel / float64(activeDaoCount)
    }
    
    // Calculate compatibility and resonance (è®¡ç®—å…¼å®¹æ€§å’Œå…±æŒ¯) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n tÆ°Æ¡ng thÃ­ch vÃ  cá»™ng hÆ°á»Ÿng
    stats["dao_compatibility"] = calculateDaoCompatibility(daoSystem.DaoCompatibility)
    stats["dao_resonance"] = calculateDaoResonance(daoSystem.DaoCompatibility)
    stats["dao_suppression"] = calculateDaoSuppression(daoSystem.DaoCompatibility)
    
    // Calculate technique stats (è®¡ç®—é“æœ¯å±æ€§) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n stats ká»¹ thuáº­t Äáº¡o
    techniqueStats := calculateDaoTechniqueStats(daoSystem.DaoTechniques)
    for key, value := range techniqueStats {
        stats[key] = value
    }
    
    return stats
}

// Calculate Profound Meaning stats (è®¡ç®—å¥¥ä¹‰å±æ€§) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n cÃ¡c stats cá»§a Ão NghÄ©a
func CalculateProfoundMeaningStats(profoundSystem ProfoundMeaningSystem) map[string]float64 {
    stats := make(map[string]float64)
    
    // Get primary Profound Meaning (è·å–ä¸»å¥¥ä¹‰) - Láº¥y Ão NghÄ©a chÃ­nh
    primaryProfound, exists := profoundSystem.ProfoundMeanings[profoundSystem.PrimaryProfoundMeaningType]
    if !exists {
        return stats // Return empty if no primary Profound Meaning (å¦‚æœæ²¡æœ‰ä¸»å¥¥ä¹‰åˆ™è¿”å›ç©º) - Náº¿u khÃ´ng cÃ³ Ão NghÄ©a chÃ­nh thÃ¬ tráº£ vá» rá»—ng
    }
    
    // Core Profound Meaning stats (æ ¸å¿ƒå¥¥ä¹‰å±æ€§) - Stats cá»‘t lÃµi Ão NghÄ©a
    stats["profound_meaning_level"] = float64(primaryProfound.MeaningLevel)
    stats["profound_meaning_experience"] = primaryProfound.MeaningExperience
    stats["profound_meaning_mastery"] = primaryProfound.MeaningMastery
    stats["profound_meaning_insight"] = primaryProfound.MeaningInsight
    stats["profound_meaning_wisdom"] = primaryProfound.MeaningWisdom
    
    // Advanced Profound Meaning stats (é«˜çº§å¥¥ä¹‰å±æ€§) - Stats nÃ¢ng cao Ão NghÄ©a
    stats["profound_meaning_harmony"] = primaryProfound.MeaningHarmony
    stats["profound_meaning_transcendence"] = primaryProfound.MeaningTranscendence
    
    // Calculate total stats across all active Profound Meanings (è®¡ç®—æ‰€æœ‰æ¿€æ´»å¥¥ä¹‰çš„æ€»å±æ€§) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n tá»•ng stats tá»« táº¥t cáº£ Ão NghÄ©a Ä‘ang hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng
    totalLevel := 0.0
    totalExperience := 0.0
    totalMastery := 0.0
    activeProfoundCount := 0
    
    for _, profound := range profoundSystem.ProfoundMeanings {
        if profound.IsActive {
            totalLevel += float64(profound.MeaningLevel)
            totalExperience += profound.MeaningExperience
            totalMastery += profound.MeaningMastery
            activeProfoundCount++
        }
    }
    
    // Average stats across active Profound Meanings (æ¿€æ´»å¥¥ä¹‰çš„å¹³å‡å±æ€§) - Stats trung bÃ¬nh cá»§a cÃ¡c Ão NghÄ©a Ä‘ang hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng
    if activeProfoundCount > 0 {
        stats["total_profound_meaning_level"] = totalLevel
        stats["total_profound_meaning_experience"] = totalExperience
        stats["total_profound_meaning_mastery"] = totalMastery
        stats["active_profound_meaning_count"] = float64(activeProfoundCount)
        stats["average_profound_meaning_level"] = totalLevel / float64(activeProfoundCount)
    }
    
    // Calculate resonance and overwhelm (è®¡ç®—å…±æŒ¯å’Œå‹å€’) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n cá»™ng hÆ°á»Ÿng vÃ  Ã¡p Ä‘áº£o
    stats["profound_meaning_resonance"] = calculateProfoundResonance(profoundSystem.ProfoundResonance)
    stats["profound_meaning_overwhelm"] = calculateProfoundOverwhelm(profoundSystem.ProfoundResonance)
    stats["profound_meaning_essence"] = calculateProfoundEssence(profoundSystem.ProfoundUnderstanding)
    
    // Calculate ability stats (è®¡ç®—å¥¥ä¹‰èƒ½åŠ›å±æ€§) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n stats kháº£ nÄƒng Ão NghÄ©a
    abilityStats := calculateProfoundAbilityStats(profoundSystem.ProfoundAbilities)
    for key, value := range abilityStats {
        stats[key] = value
    }
    
    return stats
}

// Calculate turn-based combat stats (è®¡ç®—å›åˆåˆ¶æˆ˜æ–—å±æ€§) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n stats turn-based combat
func CalculateTurnBasedCombatStats(daoSystem DaoSystem, profoundSystem ProfoundMeaningSystem) map[string]float64 {
    stats := make(map[string]float64)
    
    // Action Points calculation (è¡ŒåŠ¨ç‚¹è®¡ç®—) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n Ä‘iá»ƒm hÃ nh Ä‘á»™ng
    baseActionPoints := 3.0 // Base action points (åŸºç¡€è¡ŒåŠ¨ç‚¹) - Äiá»ƒm hÃ nh Ä‘á»™ng cÆ¡ báº£n
    daoBonus := float64(daoSystem.PrimaryDao.DaoLevel) * 0.1 // Dao bonus (é“åŠ æˆ) - Bonus tá»« Äáº¡o
    profoundBonus := float64(profoundSystem.PrimaryProfoundMeaning.MeaningLevel) * 0.05 // Profound bonus (å¥¥ä¹‰åŠ æˆ) - Bonus tá»« Ão NghÄ©a
    
    stats["action_points"] = baseActionPoints + daoBonus + profoundBonus
    stats["max_action_points"] = stats["action_points"]
    
    // Combat effectiveness calculation (æˆ˜æ–—æ•ˆæœè®¡ç®—) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n hiá»‡u quáº£ chiáº¿n Ä‘áº¥u
    daoLevel := float64(daoSystem.PrimaryDao.DaoLevel)
    profoundLevel := float64(profoundSystem.PrimaryProfoundMeaning.MeaningLevel)
    stats["combat_effectiveness"] = daoLevel * profoundLevel
    
    // Technique power calculation (é“æœ¯å¨åŠ›è®¡ç®—) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n sá»©c máº¡nh ká»¹ thuáº­t
    baseTechniquePower := 100.0 // Base technique power (åŸºç¡€é“æœ¯å¨åŠ›) - Sá»©c máº¡nh ká»¹ thuáº­t cÆ¡ báº£n
    daoMultiplier := 1.0 + (daoLevel * 0.1) // Dao multiplier (é“å€æ•°) - Há»‡ sá»‘ Äáº¡o
    profoundMultiplier := 1.0 + (profoundLevel * 0.05) // Profound multiplier (å¥¥ä¹‰å€æ•°) - Há»‡ sá»‘ Ão NghÄ©a
    
    stats["technique_power"] = baseTechniquePower * daoMultiplier * profoundMultiplier
    
    // Ability power calculation (å¥¥ä¹‰èƒ½åŠ›å¨åŠ›è®¡ç®—) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n sá»©c máº¡nh kháº£ nÄƒng Ão NghÄ©a
    baseAbilityPower := 150.0 // Base ability power (åŸºç¡€å¥¥ä¹‰èƒ½åŠ›å¨åŠ›) - Sá»©c máº¡nh kháº£ nÄƒng cÆ¡ báº£n
    stats["ability_power"] = baseAbilityPower * daoMultiplier * profoundMultiplier
    
    // Counter-attack chance calculation (åå‡»æ¦‚ç‡è®¡ç®—) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n xÃ¡c suáº¥t pháº£n cÃ´ng
    baseCounterChance := 0.1 // Base counter chance (åŸºç¡€åå‡»æ¦‚ç‡) - XÃ¡c suáº¥t pháº£n cÃ´ng cÆ¡ báº£n
    daoCounterBonus := daoLevel * 0.01 // Dao counter bonus (é“åå‡»åŠ æˆ) - Bonus pháº£n cÃ´ng tá»« Äáº¡o
    profoundCounterBonus := profoundLevel * 0.005 // Profound counter bonus (å¥¥ä¹‰åå‡»åŠ æˆ) - Bonus pháº£n cÃ´ng tá»« Ão NghÄ©a
    
    stats["counter_attack_chance"] = baseCounterChance + daoCounterBonus + profoundCounterBonus
    
    // Defensive stance effectiveness (é˜²å¾¡å§¿æ€æ•ˆæœ) - Hiá»‡u quáº£ tÆ° tháº¿ phÃ²ng thá»§
    baseDefense := 50.0 // Base defense (åŸºç¡€é˜²å¾¡) - PhÃ²ng thá»§ cÆ¡ báº£n
    daoDefenseBonus := daoLevel * 2.0 // Dao defense bonus (é“é˜²å¾¡åŠ æˆ) - Bonus phÃ²ng thá»§ tá»« Äáº¡o
    profoundDefenseBonus := profoundLevel * 1.0 // Profound defense bonus (å¥¥ä¹‰é˜²å¾¡åŠ æˆ) - Bonus phÃ²ng thá»§ tá»« Ão NghÄ©a
    
    stats["defensive_effectiveness"] = baseDefense + daoDefenseBonus + profoundDefenseBonus
    
    return stats
}

// Helper functions (è¾…åŠ©å‡½æ•°) - CÃ¡c hÃ m trá»£ giÃºp
func calculateDaoCompatibility(compatibility DaoCompatibility) float64 {
    // Calculate overall compatibility (è®¡ç®—æ€»ä½“å…¼å®¹æ€§) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n tÆ°Æ¡ng thÃ­ch tá»•ng thá»ƒ
    totalCompatibility := 0.0
    count := 0
    
    for _, innerMap := range compatibility.CompatibilityMatrix {
        for _, value := range innerMap {
            totalCompatibility += value
            count++
        }
    }
    
    if count > 0 {
        return totalCompatibility / float64(count)
    }
    return 0.0
}

func calculateDaoResonance(compatibility DaoCompatibility) float64 {
    // Calculate overall resonance (è®¡ç®—æ€»ä½“å…±æŒ¯) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n cá»™ng hÆ°á»Ÿng tá»•ng thá»ƒ
    totalResonance := 0.0
    count := 0
    
    for _, value := range compatibility.ResonanceEffects {
        totalResonance += value
        count++
    }
    
    if count > 0 {
        return totalResonance / float64(count)
    }
    return 0.0
}

func calculateDaoSuppression(compatibility DaoCompatibility) float64 {
    // Calculate overall suppression (è®¡ç®—æ€»ä½“å‹åˆ¶) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n Ã¡p cháº¿ tá»•ng thá»ƒ
    totalSuppression := 0.0
    count := 0
    
    for _, value := range compatibility.SuppressionEffects {
        totalSuppression += value
        count++
    }
    
    if count > 0 {
        return totalSuppression / float64(count)
    }
    return 0.0
}

func calculateDaoTechniqueStats(techniques []DaoTechnique) map[string]float64 {
    stats := make(map[string]float64)
    
    if len(techniques) == 0 {
        return stats
    }
    
    // Calculate average technique stats (è®¡ç®—å¹³å‡é“æœ¯å±æ€§) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n stats ká»¹ thuáº­t trung bÃ¬nh
    totalPower := 0.0
    totalCost := 0.0
    totalCooldown := 0.0
    totalRange := 0.0
    totalAccuracy := 0.0
    
    for _, technique := range techniques {
        totalPower += technique.TechniquePower
        totalCost += technique.TechniqueCost
        totalCooldown += technique.TechniqueCooldown
        totalRange += technique.TechniqueRange
        totalAccuracy += technique.TechniqueAccuracy
    }
    
    count := float64(len(techniques))
    stats["dao_technique_power"] = totalPower / count
    stats["dao_technique_cost"] = totalCost / count
    stats["dao_technique_cooldown"] = totalCooldown / count
    stats["dao_technique_range"] = totalRange / count
    stats["dao_technique_accuracy"] = totalAccuracy / count
    
    return stats
}

func calculateProfoundResonance(resonance ProfoundResonance) float64 {
    // Calculate overall resonance (è®¡ç®—æ€»ä½“å…±æŒ¯) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n cá»™ng hÆ°á»Ÿng tá»•ng thá»ƒ
    totalResonance := 0.0
    count := 0
    
    for _, value := range resonance.ResonanceEffects {
        totalResonance += value
        count++
    }
    
    if count > 0 {
        return totalResonance / float64(count)
    }
    return 0.0
}

func calculateProfoundOverwhelm(resonance ProfoundResonance) float64 {
    // Calculate overall overwhelm (è®¡ç®—æ€»ä½“å‹å€’) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n Ã¡p Ä‘áº£o tá»•ng thá»ƒ
    totalOverwhelm := 0.0
    count := 0
    
    for _, value := range resonance.OverwhelmEffects {
        totalOverwhelm += value
        count++
    }
    
    if count > 0 {
        return totalOverwhelm / float64(count)
    }
    return 0.0
}

func calculateProfoundEssence(understanding ProfoundUnderstanding) float64 {
    // Calculate profound essence (è®¡ç®—å¥¥ä¹‰æœ¬è´¨) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n báº£n cháº¥t Ão NghÄ©a
    return understanding.MeaningEssence
}

func calculateProfoundAbilityStats(abilities []ProfoundAbility) map[string]float64 {
    stats := make(map[string]float64)
    
    if len(abilities) == 0 {
        return stats
    }
    
    // Calculate average ability stats (è®¡ç®—å¹³å‡å¥¥ä¹‰èƒ½åŠ›å±æ€§) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n stats kháº£ nÄƒng trung bÃ¬nh
    totalPower := 0.0
    totalCost := 0.0
    totalCooldown := 0.0
    totalRange := 0.0
    totalAccuracy := 0.0
    
    for _, ability := range abilities {
        totalPower += ability.AbilityPower
        totalCost += ability.AbilityCost
        totalCooldown += ability.AbilityCooldown
        totalRange += ability.AbilityRange
        totalAccuracy += ability.AbilityAccuracy
    }
    
    count := float64(len(abilities))
    stats["profound_ability_power"] = totalPower / count
    stats["profound_ability_cost"] = totalCost / count
    stats["profound_ability_cooldown"] = totalCooldown / count
    stats["profound_ability_range"] = totalRange / count
    stats["profound_ability_accuracy"] = totalAccuracy / count
    
    return stats
}

// Dao and Profound Meaning Management Functions (é“å’Œå¥¥ä¹‰ç®¡ç†å‡½æ•°) - CÃ¡c hÃ m quáº£n lÃ½ Äáº¡o vÃ  Ão NghÄ©a

// Initialize Dao System (åˆå§‹åŒ–é“ç³»ç»Ÿ) - Khá»Ÿi táº¡o há»‡ thá»‘ng Äáº¡o
func InitializeDaoSystem() DaoSystem {
    return DaoSystem{
        DaoPaths: make(map[string]DaoPath),
        PrimaryDaoType: "",
        DaoComprehension: DaoComprehension{},
        DaoTechniques: make(map[string][]DaoTechnique),
        DaoCompatibility: DaoCompatibility{
            CompatibilityMatrix: make(map[string]map[string]float64),
            ResonanceEffects: make(map[string]float64),
            SuppressionEffects: make(map[string]float64),
        },
    }
}

// Initialize Profound Meaning System (åˆå§‹åŒ–å¥¥ä¹‰ç³»ç»Ÿ) - Khá»Ÿi táº¡o há»‡ thá»‘ng Ão NghÄ©a
func InitializeProfoundMeaningSystem() ProfoundMeaningSystem {
    return ProfoundMeaningSystem{
        ProfoundMeanings: make(map[string]ProfoundMeaning),
        PrimaryProfoundMeaningType: "",
        ProfoundUnderstanding: ProfoundUnderstanding{},
        ProfoundAbilities: make(map[string][]ProfoundAbility),
        ProfoundResonance: ProfoundResonance{
            ResonanceMatrix: make(map[string]map[string]float64),
            ResonanceEffects: make(map[string]float64),
            OverwhelmEffects: make(map[string]float64),
        },
    }
}

// Add Dao Path (æ·»åŠ é“å¾„) - ThÃªm con Ä‘Æ°á»ng Äáº¡o
func (ds *DaoSystem) AddDaoPath(daoType string, daoPath DaoPath) {
    daoPath.DaoType = daoType
    daoPath.IsActive = true
    daoPath.UnlockedAt = time.Now().Unix()
    
    ds.DaoPaths[daoType] = daoPath
    
    // Set as primary if it's the first one (å¦‚æœæ˜¯ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªåˆ™è®¾ä¸ºä¸»é“) - Náº¿u lÃ  cÃ¡i Ä‘áº§u tiÃªn thÃ¬ Ä‘áº·t lÃ m chÃ­nh
    if ds.PrimaryDaoType == "" {
        ds.PrimaryDaoType = daoType
        daoPath.IsPrimary = true
        ds.DaoPaths[daoType] = daoPath
    }
}

// Remove Dao Path (ç§»é™¤é“å¾„) - XÃ³a con Ä‘Æ°á»ng Äáº¡o
func (ds *DaoSystem) RemoveDaoPath(daoType string) {
    delete(ds.DaoPaths, daoType)
    
    // If removing primary Dao, set a new primary (å¦‚æœç§»é™¤ä¸»é“åˆ™è®¾ç½®æ–°çš„ä¸»é“) - Náº¿u xÃ³a Äáº¡o chÃ­nh thÃ¬ Ä‘áº·t Äáº¡o chÃ­nh má»›i
    if ds.PrimaryDaoType == daoType {
        ds.PrimaryDaoType = ""
        for daoType, dao := range ds.DaoPaths {
            if dao.IsActive {
                ds.PrimaryDaoType = daoType
                dao.IsPrimary = true
                ds.DaoPaths[daoType] = dao
                break
            }
        }
    }
}

// Set Primary Dao (è®¾ç½®ä¸»é“) - Äáº·t Äáº¡o chÃ­nh
func (ds *DaoSystem) SetPrimaryDao(daoType string) bool {
    if dao, exists := ds.DaoPaths[daoType]; exists && dao.IsActive {
        // Remove primary flag from current primary (ç§»é™¤å½“å‰ä¸»é“çš„ä¸»é“æ ‡å¿—) - XÃ³a cá» chÃ­nh khá»i Äáº¡o chÃ­nh hiá»‡n táº¡i
        if ds.PrimaryDaoType != "" {
            currentPrimary := ds.DaoPaths[ds.PrimaryDaoType]
            currentPrimary.IsPrimary = false
            ds.DaoPaths[ds.PrimaryDaoType] = currentPrimary
        }
        
        // Set new primary (è®¾ç½®æ–°ä¸»é“) - Äáº·t Äáº¡o chÃ­nh má»›i
        ds.PrimaryDaoType = daoType
        dao.IsPrimary = true
        ds.DaoPaths[daoType] = dao
        return true
    }
    return false
}

// Toggle Dao Active Status (åˆ‡æ¢é“æ¿€æ´»çŠ¶æ€) - Chuyá»ƒn Ä‘á»•i tráº¡ng thÃ¡i hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng cá»§a Äáº¡o
func (ds *DaoSystem) ToggleDaoActive(daoType string) bool {
    if dao, exists := ds.DaoPaths[daoType]; exists {
        dao.IsActive = !dao.IsActive
        ds.DaoPaths[daoType] = dao
        
        // If deactivating primary Dao, set a new primary (å¦‚æœåœç”¨ä¸»é“åˆ™è®¾ç½®æ–°çš„ä¸»é“) - Náº¿u táº¯t Äáº¡o chÃ­nh thÃ¬ Ä‘áº·t Äáº¡o chÃ­nh má»›i
        if !dao.IsActive && ds.PrimaryDaoType == daoType {
            ds.PrimaryDaoType = ""
            for daoType, dao := range ds.DaoPaths {
                if dao.IsActive {
                    ds.PrimaryDaoType = daoType
                    dao.IsPrimary = true
                    ds.DaoPaths[daoType] = dao
                    break
                }
            }
        }
        return true
    }
    return false
}

// Add Profound Meaning (æ·»åŠ å¥¥ä¹‰) - ThÃªm Ão NghÄ©a
func (pms *ProfoundMeaningSystem) AddProfoundMeaning(meaningType string, profoundMeaning ProfoundMeaning) {
    profoundMeaning.MeaningType = meaningType
    profoundMeaning.IsActive = true
    profoundMeaning.UnlockedAt = time.Now().Unix()
    
    pms.ProfoundMeanings[meaningType] = profoundMeaning
    
    // Set as primary if it's the first one (å¦‚æœæ˜¯ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªåˆ™è®¾ä¸ºä¸»å¥¥ä¹‰) - Náº¿u lÃ  cÃ¡i Ä‘áº§u tiÃªn thÃ¬ Ä‘áº·t lÃ m chÃ­nh
    if pms.PrimaryProfoundMeaningType == "" {
        pms.PrimaryProfoundMeaningType = meaningType
        profoundMeaning.IsPrimary = true
        pms.ProfoundMeanings[meaningType] = profoundMeaning
    }
}

// Remove Profound Meaning (ç§»é™¤å¥¥ä¹‰) - XÃ³a Ão NghÄ©a
func (pms *ProfoundMeaningSystem) RemoveProfoundMeaning(meaningType string) {
    delete(pms.ProfoundMeanings, meaningType)
    
    // If removing primary Profound Meaning, set a new primary (å¦‚æœç§»é™¤ä¸»å¥¥ä¹‰åˆ™è®¾ç½®æ–°çš„ä¸»å¥¥ä¹‰) - Náº¿u xÃ³a Ão NghÄ©a chÃ­nh thÃ¬ Ä‘áº·t Ão NghÄ©a chÃ­nh má»›i
    if pms.PrimaryProfoundMeaningType == meaningType {
        pms.PrimaryProfoundMeaningType = ""
        for meaningType, profound := range pms.ProfoundMeanings {
            if profound.IsActive {
                pms.PrimaryProfoundMeaningType = meaningType
                profound.IsPrimary = true
                pms.ProfoundMeanings[meaningType] = profound
                break
            }
        }
    }
}

// Set Primary Profound Meaning (è®¾ç½®ä¸»å¥¥ä¹‰) - Äáº·t Ão NghÄ©a chÃ­nh
func (pms *ProfoundMeaningSystem) SetPrimaryProfoundMeaning(meaningType string) bool {
    if profound, exists := pms.ProfoundMeanings[meaningType]; exists && profound.IsActive {
        // Remove primary flag from current primary (ç§»é™¤å½“å‰ä¸»å¥¥ä¹‰çš„ä¸»å¥¥ä¹‰æ ‡å¿—) - XÃ³a cá» chÃ­nh khá»i Ão NghÄ©a chÃ­nh hiá»‡n táº¡i
        if pms.PrimaryProfoundMeaningType != "" {
            currentPrimary := pms.ProfoundMeanings[pms.PrimaryProfoundMeaningType]
            currentPrimary.IsPrimary = false
            pms.ProfoundMeanings[pms.PrimaryProfoundMeaningType] = currentPrimary
        }
        
        // Set new primary (è®¾ç½®æ–°ä¸»å¥¥ä¹‰) - Äáº·t Ão NghÄ©a chÃ­nh má»›i
        pms.PrimaryProfoundMeaningType = meaningType
        profound.IsPrimary = true
        pms.ProfoundMeanings[meaningType] = profound
        return true
    }
    return false
}

// Toggle Profound Meaning Active Status (åˆ‡æ¢å¥¥ä¹‰æ¿€æ´»çŠ¶æ€) - Chuyá»ƒn Ä‘á»•i tráº¡ng thÃ¡i hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng cá»§a Ão NghÄ©a
func (pms *ProfoundMeaningSystem) ToggleProfoundMeaningActive(meaningType string) bool {
    if profound, exists := pms.ProfoundMeanings[meaningType]; exists {
        profound.IsActive = !profound.IsActive
        pms.ProfoundMeanings[meaningType] = profound
        
        // If deactivating primary Profound Meaning, set a new primary (å¦‚æœåœç”¨ä¸»å¥¥ä¹‰åˆ™è®¾ç½®æ–°çš„ä¸»å¥¥ä¹‰) - Náº¿u táº¯t Ão NghÄ©a chÃ­nh thÃ¬ Ä‘áº·t Ão NghÄ©a chÃ­nh má»›i
        if !profound.IsActive && pms.PrimaryProfoundMeaningType == meaningType {
            pms.PrimaryProfoundMeaningType = ""
            for meaningType, profound := range pms.ProfoundMeanings {
                if profound.IsActive {
                    pms.PrimaryProfoundMeaningType = meaningType
                    profound.IsPrimary = true
                    pms.ProfoundMeanings[meaningType] = profound
                    break
                }
            }
        }
        return true
    }
    return false
}

// Get Active Daos (è·å–æ¿€æ´»çš„é“) - Láº¥y cÃ¡c Äáº¡o Ä‘ang hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng
func (ds *DaoSystem) GetActiveDaos() []DaoPath {
    var activeDaos []DaoPath
    for _, dao := range ds.DaoPaths {
        if dao.IsActive {
            activeDaos = append(activeDaos, dao)
        }
    }
    return activeDaos
}

// Get Active Profound Meanings (è·å–æ¿€æ´»çš„å¥¥ä¹‰) - Láº¥y cÃ¡c Ão NghÄ©a Ä‘ang hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng
func (pms *ProfoundMeaningSystem) GetActiveProfoundMeanings() []ProfoundMeaning {
    var activeProfoundMeanings []ProfoundMeaning
    for _, profound := range pms.ProfoundMeanings {
        if profound.IsActive {
            activeProfoundMeanings = append(activeProfoundMeanings, profound)
        }
    }
    return activeProfoundMeanings
}

// Get Dao by Type (æ ¹æ®ç±»å‹è·å–é“) - Láº¥y Äáº¡o theo loáº¡i
func (ds *DaoSystem) GetDaoByType(daoType string) (DaoPath, bool) {
    dao, exists := ds.DaoPaths[daoType]
    return dao, exists
}

// Get Profound Meaning by Type (æ ¹æ®ç±»å‹è·å–å¥¥ä¹‰) - Láº¥y Ão NghÄ©a theo loáº¡i
func (pms *ProfoundMeaningSystem) GetProfoundMeaningByType(meaningType string) (ProfoundMeaning, bool) {
    profound, exists := pms.ProfoundMeanings[meaningType]
    return profound, exists
}
```

#### **F. VÃ­ Dá»¥ Sá»­ Dá»¥ng (Usage Examples):**

```go
// Example: Creating a multi-Dao cultivator (ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼šåˆ›å»ºå¤šé“ä¿®ç‚¼è€…) - VÃ­ dá»¥: Táº¡o má»™t tu luyá»‡n giáº£ Ä‘a Äáº¡o
func ExampleMultiDaoCultivator() {
    // Initialize systems (åˆå§‹åŒ–ç³»ç»Ÿ) - Khá»Ÿi táº¡o há»‡ thá»‘ng
    daoSystem := InitializeDaoSystem()
    profoundSystem := InitializeProfoundMeaningSystem()
    
    // Add Sword Dao as primary (æ·»åŠ å‰‘é“ä½œä¸ºä¸»é“) - ThÃªm Kiáº¿m Äáº¡o lÃ m chÃ­nh
    swordDao := DaoPath{
        DaoLevel: 5,
        DaoExperience: 1000.0,
        DaoMastery: 0.8,
        DaoInsight: 0.7,
        DaoWisdom: 0.6,
        DaoHarmony: 0.5,
        DaoTranscendence: 0.3,
    }
    daoSystem.AddDaoPath(DaoTypeSword, swordDao)
    
    // Add Blade Dao as secondary (æ·»åŠ åˆ€é“ä½œä¸ºå‰¯é“) - ThÃªm Äao Äáº¡o lÃ m phá»¥
    bladeDao := DaoPath{
        DaoLevel: 3,
        DaoExperience: 500.0,
        DaoMastery: 0.6,
        DaoInsight: 0.5,
        DaoWisdom: 0.4,
        DaoHarmony: 0.3,
        DaoTranscendence: 0.1,
    }
    daoSystem.AddDaoPath(DaoTypeBlade, bladeDao)
    
    // Add Spell Dao as secondary (æ·»åŠ æ³•é“ä½œä¸ºå‰¯é“) - ThÃªm PhÃ¡p Äáº¡o lÃ m phá»¥
    spellDao := DaoPath{
        DaoLevel: 2,
        DaoExperience: 200.0,
        DaoMastery: 0.4,
        DaoInsight: 0.6,
        DaoWisdom: 0.7,
        DaoHarmony: 0.2,
        DaoTranscendence: 0.1,
    }
    daoSystem.AddDaoPath(DaoTypeSpell, spellDao)
    
    // Add Sword Intent as primary Profound Meaning (æ·»åŠ å‰‘æ„ä½œä¸ºä¸»å¥¥ä¹‰) - ThÃªm Kiáº¿m Ã lÃ m Ão NghÄ©a chÃ­nh
    swordIntent := ProfoundMeaning{
        MeaningLevel: 4,
        MeaningExperience: 800.0,
        MeaningMastery: 0.7,
        MeaningInsight: 0.6,
        MeaningWisdom: 0.5,
        MeaningHarmony: 0.4,
        MeaningTranscendence: 0.2,
    }
    profoundSystem.AddProfoundMeaning(ProfoundMeaningTypeSwordIntent, swordIntent)
    
    // Add Blade Intent as secondary (æ·»åŠ åˆ€æ„ä½œä¸ºå‰¯å¥¥ä¹‰) - ThÃªm Äao Ã lÃ m phá»¥
    bladeIntent := ProfoundMeaning{
        MeaningLevel: 2,
        MeaningExperience: 300.0,
        MeaningMastery: 0.5,
        MeaningInsight: 0.4,
        MeaningWisdom: 0.3,
        MeaningHarmony: 0.2,
        MeaningTranscendence: 0.1,
    }
    profoundSystem.AddProfoundMeaning(ProfoundMeaningTypeBladeIntent, bladeIntent)
    
    // Calculate stats (è®¡ç®—å±æ€§) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n stats
    daoStats := CalculateDaoStats(daoSystem)
    profoundStats := CalculateProfoundMeaningStats(profoundSystem)
    combatStats := CalculateTurnBasedCombatStats(daoSystem, profoundSystem)
    
    // Print results (æ‰“å°ç»“æœ) - In káº¿t quáº£
    fmt.Printf("Primary Dao: %s (Level %d)\n", daoSystem.PrimaryDaoType, int(daoStats["dao_level"]))
    fmt.Printf("Active Daos: %d\n", int(daoStats["active_dao_count"]))
    fmt.Printf("Total Dao Level: %.1f\n", daoStats["total_dao_level"])
    fmt.Printf("Average Dao Level: %.1f\n", daoStats["average_dao_level"])
    
    fmt.Printf("Primary Profound Meaning: %s (Level %d)\n", profoundSystem.PrimaryProfoundMeaningType, int(profoundStats["profound_meaning_level"]))
    fmt.Printf("Active Profound Meanings: %d\n", int(profoundStats["active_profound_meaning_count"]))
    fmt.Printf("Total Profound Meaning Level: %.1f\n", profoundStats["total_profound_meaning_level"])
    
    fmt.Printf("Action Points: %.1f\n", combatStats["action_points"])
    fmt.Printf("Combat Effectiveness: %.1f\n", combatStats["combat_effectiveness"])
    fmt.Printf("Technique Power: %.1f\n", combatStats["technique_power"])
    fmt.Printf("Counter Attack Chance: %.2f\n", combatStats["counter_attack_chance"])
}

// Example: Switching primary Dao (ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼šåˆ‡æ¢ä¸»é“) - VÃ­ dá»¥: Chuyá»ƒn Ä‘á»•i Äáº¡o chÃ­nh
func ExampleSwitchPrimaryDao() {
    daoSystem := InitializeDaoSystem()
    
    // Add multiple Daos (æ·»åŠ å¤šä¸ªé“) - ThÃªm nhiá»u Äáº¡o
    daoSystem.AddDaoPath(DaoTypeSword, DaoPath{DaoLevel: 5, DaoMastery: 0.8})
    daoSystem.AddDaoPath(DaoTypeBlade, DaoPath{DaoLevel: 3, DaoMastery: 0.6})
    daoSystem.AddDaoPath(DaoTypeSpell, DaoPath{DaoLevel: 7, DaoMastery: 0.9})
    
    // Initially Sword Dao is primary (æœ€åˆå‰‘é“æ˜¯ä¸»é“) - Ban Ä‘áº§u Kiáº¿m Äáº¡o lÃ  chÃ­nh
    fmt.Printf("Primary Dao: %s\n", daoSystem.PrimaryDaoType) // "sword_dao"
    
    // Switch to Spell Dao as primary (åˆ‡æ¢åˆ°æ³•é“ä½œä¸ºä¸»é“) - Chuyá»ƒn sang PhÃ¡p Äáº¡o lÃ m chÃ­nh
    success := daoSystem.SetPrimaryDao(DaoTypeSpell)
    if success {
        fmt.Printf("Primary Dao changed to: %s\n", daoSystem.PrimaryDaoType) // "spell_dao"
    }
}

// Example: Toggle Dao active status (ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼šåˆ‡æ¢é“æ¿€æ´»çŠ¶æ€) - VÃ­ dá»¥: Chuyá»ƒn Ä‘á»•i tráº¡ng thÃ¡i hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng cá»§a Äáº¡o
func ExampleToggleDaoActive() {
    daoSystem := InitializeDaoSystem()
    
    // Add multiple Daos (æ·»åŠ å¤šä¸ªé“) - ThÃªm nhiá»u Äáº¡o
    daoSystem.AddDaoPath(DaoTypeSword, DaoPath{DaoLevel: 5})
    daoSystem.AddDaoPath(DaoTypeBlade, DaoPath{DaoLevel: 3})
    daoSystem.AddDaoPath(DaoTypeSpell, DaoPath{DaoLevel: 7})
    
    // Deactivate Blade Dao (åœç”¨åˆ€é“) - Táº¯t Äao Äáº¡o
    daoSystem.ToggleDaoActive(DaoTypeBlade)
    
    // Get active Daos (è·å–æ¿€æ´»çš„é“) - Láº¥y cÃ¡c Äáº¡o Ä‘ang hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng
    activeDaos := daoSystem.GetActiveDaos()
    fmt.Printf("Active Daos: %d\n", len(activeDaos)) // 2 (Sword and Spell)
    
    // Reactivate Blade Dao (é‡æ–°æ¿€æ´»åˆ€é“) - Báº­t láº¡i Äao Äáº¡o
    daoSystem.ToggleDaoActive(DaoTypeBlade)
    activeDaos = daoSystem.GetActiveDaos()
    fmt.Printf("Active Daos after reactivation: %d\n", len(activeDaos)) // 3 (All)
}

// Example: Adding new Dao types dynamically (ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼šåŠ¨æ€æ·»åŠ æ–°é“ç±»å‹) - VÃ­ dá»¥: ThÃªm loáº¡i Äáº¡o má»›i Ä‘á»™ng
func ExampleAddNewDaoType() {
    daoSystem := InitializeDaoSystem()
    
    // Add existing Daos (æ·»åŠ ç°æœ‰é“) - ThÃªm cÃ¡c Äáº¡o hiá»‡n cÃ³
    daoSystem.AddDaoPath(DaoTypeSword, DaoPath{DaoLevel: 5})
    daoSystem.AddDaoPath(DaoTypeBlade, DaoPath{DaoLevel: 3})
    
    // Add new custom Dao type (æ·»åŠ æ–°çš„è‡ªå®šä¹‰é“ç±»å‹) - ThÃªm loáº¡i Äáº¡o tÃ¹y chá»‰nh má»›i
    customDaoType := "lightning_dao" // Lightning Dao (é›·é“) - LÃ´i Äáº¡o
    lightningDao := DaoPath{
        DaoLevel: 4,
        DaoExperience: 600.0,
        DaoMastery: 0.7,
        DaoInsight: 0.8,
        DaoWisdom: 0.5,
        DaoHarmony: 0.6,
        DaoTranscendence: 0.3,
    }
    daoSystem.AddDaoPath(customDaoType, lightningDao)
    
    // The system automatically handles the new type (ç³»ç»Ÿè‡ªåŠ¨å¤„ç†æ–°ç±»å‹) - Há»‡ thá»‘ng tá»± Ä‘á»™ng xá»­ lÃ½ loáº¡i má»›i
    fmt.Printf("Total Daos: %d\n", len(daoSystem.DaoPaths)) // 3
    fmt.Printf("Custom Dao Level: %d\n", daoSystem.DaoPaths[customDaoType].DaoLevel) // 4
}
```

#### **E. TÃ­ch Há»£p Vá»›i Actor Core v3:**

```go
// Convert Dao and Profound Meaning to SubsystemOutput (è½¬æ¢é“å’Œå¥¥ä¹‰åˆ°å­ç³»ç»Ÿè¾“å‡º) - Chuyá»ƒn Ä‘á»•i Äáº¡o vÃ  Ão NghÄ©a thÃ nh SubsystemOutput
func ConvertDaoAndProfoundToSubsystemOutput(daoSystem DaoSystem, profoundSystem ProfoundMeaningSystem) SubsystemOutput {
    // Calculate primary stats (è®¡ç®—ä¸»è¦å±æ€§) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n primary stats
    daoStats := CalculateDaoStats(daoSystem)
    profoundStats := CalculateProfoundMeaningStats(profoundSystem)
    combatStats := CalculateTurnBasedCombatStats(daoSystem, profoundSystem)
    
    // Combine all primary stats (åˆå¹¶æ‰€æœ‰ä¸»è¦å±æ€§) - Káº¿t há»£p táº¥t cáº£ primary stats
    primaryStats := make(map[string]float64)
    for key, value := range daoStats {
        primaryStats[key] = value
    }
    for key, value := range profoundStats {
        primaryStats[key] = value
    }
    for key, value := range combatStats {
        primaryStats[key] = value
    }
    
    // Calculate derived stats (è®¡ç®—æ´¾ç”Ÿå±æ€§) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n derived stats
    derivedStats := make(map[string]float64)
    
    // Combat effectiveness derived stats (æˆ˜æ–—æ•ˆæœæ´¾ç”Ÿå±æ€§) - Derived stats hiá»‡u quáº£ chiáº¿n Ä‘áº¥u
    derivedStats["total_combat_power"] = primaryStats["combat_effectiveness"] * primaryStats["technique_power"]
    derivedStats["total_ability_power"] = primaryStats["combat_effectiveness"] * primaryStats["ability_power"]
    derivedStats["total_defensive_power"] = primaryStats["defensive_effectiveness"] * primaryStats["dao_harmony"]
    
    // Action economy derived stats (è¡ŒåŠ¨ç»æµæ´¾ç”Ÿå±æ€§) - Derived stats kinh táº¿ hÃ nh Ä‘á»™ng
    derivedStats["action_efficiency"] = primaryStats["action_points"] * primaryStats["dao_mastery"]
    derivedStats["technique_efficiency"] = primaryStats["dao_technique_power"] / primaryStats["dao_technique_cost"]
    derivedStats["ability_efficiency"] = primaryStats["profound_ability_power"] / primaryStats["profound_ability_cost"]
    
    // Create contributions (åˆ›å»ºè´¡çŒ®) - Táº¡o contributions
    var contributions []Contribution
    
    // Primary stats contributions (ä¸»è¦å±æ€§è´¡çŒ®) - Contributions primary stats
    for stat, value := range primaryStats {
        contributions = append(contributions, Contribution{
            Dimension: stat,
            Bucket:    "Primary",
            Value:     value,
            System:    "DaoProfoundSystem",
            Priority:  1,
        })
    }
    
    // Derived stats contributions (æ´¾ç”Ÿå±æ€§è´¡çŒ®) - Contributions derived stats
    for stat, value := range derivedStats {
        contributions = append(contributions, Contribution{
            Dimension: stat,
            Bucket:    "Derived",
            Value:     value,
            System:    "DaoProfoundSystem",
            Priority:  2,
        })
    }
    
    // Caps contributions (ä¸Šé™è´¡çŒ®) - Contributions caps
    caps := make(map[string]float64)
    caps["max_dao_level"] = 15.0 // Maximum Dao level (æœ€å¤§é“ç­‰çº§) - Cáº¥p Ä‘á»™ Äáº¡o tá»‘i Ä‘a
    caps["max_profound_meaning_level"] = 10.0 // Maximum Profound Meaning level (æœ€å¤§å¥¥ä¹‰ç­‰çº§) - Cáº¥p Ä‘á»™ Ão NghÄ©a tá»‘i Ä‘a
    caps["max_action_points"] = 10.0 // Maximum action points (æœ€å¤§è¡ŒåŠ¨ç‚¹) - Äiá»ƒm hÃ nh Ä‘á»™ng tá»‘i Ä‘a
    
    for stat, value := range caps {
        contributions = append(contributions, Contribution{
            Dimension: stat,
            Bucket:    "Caps",
            Value:     value,
            System:    "DaoProfoundSystem",
            Priority:  3,
        })
    }
    
    return SubsystemOutput{
        Primary:   primaryStats,
        Derived:   derivedStats,
        Caps:      caps,
        Context:   map[string]interface{}{"dao_system": daoSystem, "profound_system": profoundSystem},
        Contributions: contributions,
    }
}
```

### **1. Äan Äiá»n (Dantian) - KhÃ­ Quan Chá»©a KhÃ­**
Äan Ä‘iá»n lÃ  trung tÃ¢m lÆ°u trá»¯ vÃ  chuyá»ƒn hÃ³a khÃ­, áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng Ä‘áº¿n cÃ¡c primary stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n **KhÃ­**:

#### **Primary Stats tá»« Äan Äiá»n:**
```go
// Dantian-related primary stats (ä¸¹ç”°ç›¸å…³ä¸»è¦å±æ€§) - CÃ¡c primary stats tá»« Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
var DantianPrimaryStats = []string{
    "dantian_capacity",        // Dantian capacity (ä¸¹ç”°å®¹é‡) - Dung lÆ°á»£ng Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
    "dantian_compression",     // Dantian compression (ä¸¹ç”°å‹ç¼©) - Suáº¥t nÃ©n khÃ­ trong Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
    "dantian_stability",       // Dantian stability (ä¸¹ç”°ç¨³å®šæ€§) - Äá»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
    "dantian_purity",          // Dantian purity (ä¸¹ç”°çº¯åº¦) - Äá»™ tinh khiáº¿t Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
    "qi_purity",              // Qi purity (æ°”çº¯åº¦) - Äá»™ tinh khiáº¿t khÃ­
    "eff_jing_to_qi",         // Jing to Qi efficiency (ç²¾è½¬æ°”æ•ˆç‡) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t chuyá»ƒn Tinh â†’ KhÃ­
    "eff_qi_to_shen",         // Qi to Shen efficiency (æ°”è½¬ç¥æ•ˆç‡) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t chuyá»ƒn KhÃ­ â†’ Tháº§n
    "cultivation_exp",         // Main cultivation experience (ä¸»è¦ä¿®ç‚¼ç»éªŒ) - Tu vi chÃ­nh
    "aux_cultivation_exp",     // Auxiliary cultivation experience (è¾…åŠ©ä¿®ç‚¼ç»éªŒ) - Tu vi phá»¥
    "total_cultivation_exp",   // Total cultivation experience (æ€»ä¿®ç‚¼ç»éªŒ) - Tu vi tá»•ng há»£p
}
```

#### **CÃ´ng Thá»©c TÃ­nh ToÃ¡n Äan Äiá»n:**
```go
// Calculate dantian-related stats (è®¡ç®—ä¸¹ç”°ç›¸å…³å±æ€§) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n cÃ¡c stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
func CalculateDantianStats(dantian DantianInfo) map[string]float64 {
    stats := make(map[string]float64)
    
    // Dantian capacity (ä¸¹ç”°å®¹é‡) - Dung lÆ°á»£ng Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
    stats["dantian_capacity"] = dantian.Storage.DantianCapacity
    
    // Dantian compression (ä¸¹ç”°å‹ç¼©) - Suáº¥t nÃ©n khÃ­ = Tu vi / Dung lÆ°á»£ng
    stats["dantian_compression"] = dantian.Core.TotalCultivationExp / dantian.Storage.DantianCapacity
    
    // Dantian stability (ä¸¹ç”°ç¨³å®šæ€§) - Äá»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
    stats["dantian_stability"] = dantian.Quality.DantianStability
    
    // Dantian purity (ä¸¹ç”°çº¯åº¦) - Äá»™ tinh khiáº¿t Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
    stats["dantian_purity"] = dantian.Quality.DantianPurity
    
    // Qi purity (æ°”çº¯åº¦) - Äá»™ tinh khiáº¿t khÃ­ = Äá»™ tinh khiáº¿t Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n * 0.8 + Äá»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh * 0.2
    stats["qi_purity"] = dantian.Quality.DantianPurity*0.8 + dantian.Quality.DantianStability*0.2
    
    // Jing to Qi efficiency (ç²¾è½¬æ°”æ•ˆç‡) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t chuyá»ƒn Tinh â†’ KhÃ­ = Äá»™ tinh khiáº¿t * 0.6 + Äá»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh * 0.4
    stats["eff_jing_to_qi"] = dantian.Quality.DantianPurity*0.6 + dantian.Quality.DantianStability*0.4
    
    // Qi to Shen efficiency (æ°”è½¬ç¥æ•ˆç‡) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t chuyá»ƒn KhÃ­ â†’ Tháº§n = Äá»™ tinh khiáº¿t * 0.4 + Äá»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh * 0.6
    stats["eff_qi_to_shen"] = dantian.Quality.DantianPurity*0.4 + dantian.Quality.DantianStability*0.6
    
    // Cultivation experience (ä¿®ç‚¼ç»éªŒ) - Tu vi
    stats["cultivation_exp"] = dantian.Core.CultivationExp
    stats["aux_cultivation_exp"] = dantian.Core.AuxCultivationExp
    stats["total_cultivation_exp"] = dantian.Core.TotalCultivationExp
    
    return stats
}
```

### **2. Kinh Máº¡ch (Meridians) - Há»‡ Thá»‘ng Váº­n Chuyá»ƒn KhÃ­**
Kinh máº¡ch lÃ  há»‡ thá»‘ng váº­n chuyá»ƒn khÃ­ trong cÆ¡ thá»ƒ, áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng Ä‘áº¿n cÃ¡c primary stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n **váº­n chuyá»ƒn vÃ  lÆ°u thÃ´ng khÃ­**:

#### **Primary Stats tá»« Kinh Máº¡ch:**

}

#### **Primary Stats áº¢nh HÆ°á»Ÿng Bá»Ÿi Kinh Máº¡ch:**

```go
// Meridian-related primary stats (ç»è„‰ç›¸å…³ä¸»è¦å±æ€§) - CÃ¡c primary stats tá»« kinh máº¡ch
var MeridianPrimaryStats = []string{
    // Core meridian stats (æ ¸å¿ƒç»è„‰å±æ€§) - Stats cá»‘t lÃµi kinh máº¡ch
    "meridian_conductivity",      // Meridian conductivity (ç»è„‰ä¼ å¯¼æ€§) - Äá»™ dáº«n khÃ­ trong kinh máº¡ch
    "meridian_toughness",         // Meridian toughness (ç»è„‰éŸ§æ€§) - Sá»©c chá»‹u Ã¡p lá»±c khÃ­
    "meridian_purity_resistance", // Meridian purity resistance (ç»è„‰å‡€æŠ—æ€§) - Chá»‘ng táº¡p cháº¥t bÃ¡m lÆ°u
    "meridian_flexibility",       // Meridian flexibility (ç»è„‰æŸ”éŸ§æ€§) - Äá»™ linh hoáº¡t kinh máº¡ch
    "meridian_resilience",        // Meridian resilience (ç»è„‰æ¢å¤åŠ›) - Kháº£ nÄƒng phá»¥c há»“i kinh máº¡ch
    
    // Capacity and flow stats (å®¹é‡å’ŒæµåŠ¨å±æ€§) - Stats dung lÆ°á»£ng vÃ  dÃ²ng cháº£y
    "meridian_capacity",          // Meridian capacity (ç»è„‰å®¹é‡) - Dung lÆ°á»£ng kinh máº¡ch
    "meridian_flow_rate",         // Meridian flow rate (ç»è„‰æµé€Ÿ) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ dÃ²ng cháº£y
    "meridian_pressure",          // Meridian pressure (ç»è„‰å‹åŠ›) - Ãp lá»±c kinh máº¡ch
    "meridian_efficiency",        // Meridian efficiency (ç»è„‰æ•ˆç‡) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t váº­n chuyá»ƒn khÃ­
    "meridian_flow_efficiency",   // Meridian flow efficiency (ç»è„‰æµåŠ¨æ•ˆç‡) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t dÃ²ng cháº£y
    
    // Jing-related stats (ç²¾ç›¸å…³å±æ€§) - Stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n Tinh
    "jing_reserve",              // Jing reserve (ç²¾å‚¨å¤‡) - Dá»± trá»¯ Tinh (nguyÃªn khÃ­)
    "jing_regeneration",         // Jing regeneration (ç²¾æ¢å¤) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ há»“i tinh
    "jing_consumption",          // Jing consumption (ç²¾æ¶ˆè€—) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ tiÃªu hao tinh
    "jing_efficiency",           // Jing efficiency (ç²¾æ•ˆç‡) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t sá»­ dá»¥ng tinh
    
    // Channel-specific stats (é€šé“ç‰¹å®šå±æ€§) - Stats Ä‘áº·c thÃ¹ kÃªnh
    "main_channel_health",       // Main channel health (ä¸»è„‰å¥åº·åº¦) - Sá»©c khá»e kÃªnh chÃ­nh
    "secondary_channel_health",  // Secondary channel health (æ”¯è„‰å¥åº·åº¦) - Sá»©c khá»e kÃªnh phá»¥
    "micro_channel_health",      // Micro channel health (å¾®è„‰å¥åº·åº¦) - Sá»©c khá»e kÃªnh vi mÃ´
    "channel_balance",           // Channel balance (é€šé“å¹³è¡¡) - CÃ¢n báº±ng kÃªnh
    "channel_synchronization",   // Channel synchronization (é€šé“åŒæ­¥) - Äá»“ng bá»™ kÃªnh
    
    // Cultivation-related stats (ä¿®ç‚¼ç›¸å…³å±æ€§) - Stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n tu luyá»‡n
    "meridian_cultivation_level", // Meridian cultivation level (ç»è„‰ä¿®ç‚¼ç­‰çº§) - Cáº¥p Ä‘á»™ tu luyá»‡n kinh máº¡ch
    "meridian_cultivation_exp",   // Meridian cultivation exp (ç»è„‰ä¿®ç‚¼ç»éªŒ) - Kinh nghiá»‡m tu luyá»‡n kinh máº¡ch
    "meridian_cultivation_speed", // Meridian cultivation speed (ç»è„‰ä¿®ç‚¼é€Ÿåº¦) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ tu luyá»‡n kinh máº¡ch
    "meridian_breakthrough_chance", // Meridian breakthrough chance (ç»è„‰çªç ´å‡ ç‡) - Tá»· lá»‡ Ä‘á»™t phÃ¡ kinh máº¡ch
    "meridian_stability",         // Meridian stability (ç»è„‰ç¨³å®šæ€§) - Äá»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh kinh máº¡ch
}
```

#### **CÃ´ng Thá»©c TÃ­nh ToÃ¡n Kinh Máº¡ch Chi Tiáº¿t:**
```go
// Calculate meridian-related stats (è®¡ç®—ç»è„‰ç›¸å…³å±æ€§) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n cÃ¡c stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n kinh máº¡ch
func CalculateMeridianStats(meridians MeridianSystem) map[string]float64 {
    stats := make(map[string]float64)
    
    // Core meridian stats (æ ¸å¿ƒç»è„‰å±æ€§) - Stats cá»‘t lÃµi kinh máº¡ch
    stats["meridian_conductivity"] = meridians.MeridianQuality.Conductivity
    stats["meridian_toughness"] = meridians.MeridianQuality.Toughness
    stats["meridian_purity_resistance"] = meridians.MeridianQuality.PurityResistance
    stats["meridian_flexibility"] = meridians.MeridianQuality.Flexibility
    stats["meridian_resilience"] = meridians.MeridianQuality.Resilience
    
    // Capacity and flow stats (å®¹é‡å’ŒæµåŠ¨å±æ€§) - Stats dung lÆ°á»£ng vÃ  dÃ²ng cháº£y
    stats["meridian_capacity"] = meridians.MeridianCapacity.TotalCapacity
    stats["meridian_flow_rate"] = meridians.MeridianCapacity.MaxFlowRate
    stats["meridian_pressure"] = meridians.MeridianCapacity.MaxPressure
    stats["meridian_efficiency"] = (meridians.MeridianQuality.Conductivity + meridians.MeridianQuality.Toughness) / 2.0
    stats["meridian_flow_efficiency"] = meridians.MeridianCapacity.FlowEfficiency
    
    // Jing-related stats (ç²¾ç›¸å…³å±æ€§) - Stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n Tinh
    stats["jing_reserve"] = meridians.JingReserve.TotalJing
    stats["jing_regeneration"] = meridians.JingReserve.JingRegeneration
    stats["jing_consumption"] = meridians.JingReserve.JingConsumption
    stats["jing_efficiency"] = meridians.JingReserve.JingEfficiency
    
    // Channel-specific stats (é€šé“ç‰¹å®šå±æ€§) - Stats Ä‘áº·c thÃ¹ kÃªnh
    stats["main_channel_health"] = CalculateMainChannelHealth(meridians.MeridianChannels.MainChannels)
    stats["secondary_channel_health"] = CalculateSecondaryChannelHealth(meridians.MeridianChannels.SecondaryChannels)
    stats["micro_channel_health"] = CalculateMicroChannelHealth(meridians.MeridianChannels.MicroChannels)
    stats["channel_balance"] = CalculateChannelBalance(meridians.MeridianChannels)
    stats["channel_synchronization"] = CalculateChannelSynchronization(meridians.MeridianChannels)
    
    // Cultivation-related stats (ä¿®ç‚¼ç›¸å…³å±æ€§) - Stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n tu luyá»‡n
    stats["meridian_cultivation_level"] = float64(meridians.MeridianCultivation.CultivationLevel)
    stats["meridian_cultivation_exp"] = meridians.MeridianCultivation.CultivationExp
    stats["meridian_cultivation_speed"] = meridians.MeridianCultivation.CultivationSpeed
    stats["meridian_breakthrough_chance"] = meridians.MeridianCultivation.BreakthroughChance
    stats["meridian_stability"] = meridians.MeridianCultivation.MeridianStability
    
    return stats
}

// Calculate main channel health (è®¡ç®—ä¸»è„‰å¥åº·åº¦) - TÃ­nh sá»©c khá»e kÃªnh chÃ­nh
func CalculateMainChannelHealth(mainChannels MainChannels) float64 {
    channels := []MeridianChannel{
        mainChannels.HandTaiyinLung,
        mainChannels.HandYangmingLargeIntestine,
        mainChannels.HandShaoyinHeart,
        mainChannels.HandTaiyangSmallIntestine,
        mainChannels.HandJueyinPericardium,
        mainChannels.HandShaoyangTripleBurner,
        mainChannels.FootTaiyinSpleen,
        mainChannels.FootYangmingStomach,
        mainChannels.FootShaoyinKidney,
        mainChannels.FootTaiyangBladder,
        mainChannels.FootJueyinLiver,
        mainChannels.FootShaoyangGallbladder,
    }
    
    totalHealth := 0.0
    for _, channel := range channels {
        totalHealth += channel.ChannelHealth
    }
    
    return totalHealth / float64(len(channels))
}

// Calculate secondary channel health (è®¡ç®—æ”¯è„‰å¥åº·åº¦) - TÃ­nh sá»©c khá»e kÃªnh phá»¥
func CalculateSecondaryChannelHealth(secondaryChannels SecondaryChannels) float64 {
    allChannels := append(secondaryChannels.CollateralChannels, secondaryChannels.DivergentChannels...)
    allChannels = append(allChannels, secondaryChannels.MuscleChannels...)
    allChannels = append(allChannels, secondaryChannels.SkinChannels...)
    
    if len(allChannels) == 0 {
        return 0.0
    }
    
    totalHealth := 0.0
    for _, channel := range allChannels {
        totalHealth += channel.ChannelHealth
    }
    
    return totalHealth / float64(len(allChannels))
}

// Calculate micro channel health (è®¡ç®—å¾®è„‰å¥åº·åº¦) - TÃ­nh sá»©c khá»e kÃªnh vi mÃ´
func CalculateMicroChannelHealth(microChannels MicroChannels) float64 {
    allChannels := append(microChannels.CapillaryChannels, microChannels.NerveChannels...)
    allChannels = append(allChannels, microChannels.EnergyChannels...)
    
    if len(allChannels) == 0 {
        return 0.0
    }
    
    totalHealth := 0.0
    for _, channel := range allChannels {
        totalHealth += channel.ChannelHealth
    }
    
    return totalHealth / float64(len(allChannels))
}

// Calculate channel balance (è®¡ç®—é€šé“å¹³è¡¡) - TÃ­nh cÃ¢n báº±ng kÃªnh
func CalculateChannelBalance(channels MeridianChannels) float64 {
    mainHealth := CalculateMainChannelHealth(channels.MainChannels)
    secondaryHealth := CalculateSecondaryChannelHealth(channels.SecondaryChannels)
    microHealth := CalculateMicroChannelHealth(channels.MicroChannels)
    
    // Balance = 1 - (max - min) / max
    maxHealth := mainHealth
    minHealth := mainHealth
    
    if secondaryHealth > maxHealth {
        maxHealth = secondaryHealth
    }
    if microHealth > maxHealth {
        maxHealth = microHealth
    }
    
    if secondaryHealth < minHealth {
        minHealth = secondaryHealth
    }
    if microHealth < minHealth {
        minHealth = microHealth
    }
    
    if maxHealth == 0 {
        return 0.0
    }
    
    return 1.0 - (maxHealth - minHealth) / maxHealth
}

// Calculate channel synchronization (è®¡ç®—é€šé“åŒæ­¥) - TÃ­nh Ä‘á»“ng bá»™ kÃªnh
func CalculateChannelSynchronization(channels MeridianChannels) float64 {
    // Synchronization based on flow consistency across channels
    // Äá»“ng bá»™ dá»±a trÃªn tÃ­nh nháº¥t quÃ¡n dÃ²ng cháº£y qua cÃ¡c kÃªnh
    mainChannels := []MeridianChannel{
        channels.MainChannels.HandTaiyinLung,
        channels.MainChannels.HandYangmingLargeIntestine,
        channels.MainChannels.HandShaoyinHeart,
        channels.MainChannels.HandTaiyangSmallIntestine,
        channels.MainChannels.HandJueyinPericardium,
        channels.MainChannels.HandShaoyangTripleBurner,
        channels.MainChannels.FootTaiyinSpleen,
        channels.MainChannels.FootYangmingStomach,
        channels.MainChannels.FootShaoyinKidney,
        channels.MainChannels.FootTaiyangBladder,
        channels.MainChannels.FootJueyinLiver,
        channels.MainChannels.FootShaoyangGallbladder,
    }
    
    if len(mainChannels) == 0 {
        return 0.0
    }
    
    // Calculate flow variance (è®¡ç®—æµé‡æ–¹å·®) - TÃ­nh phÆ°Æ¡ng sai dÃ²ng cháº£y
    totalFlow := 0.0
    for _, channel := range mainChannels {
        totalFlow += channel.ChannelFlow
    }
    
    avgFlow := totalFlow / float64(len(mainChannels))
    
    variance := 0.0
    for _, channel := range mainChannels {
        diff := channel.ChannelFlow - avgFlow
        variance += diff * diff
    }
    
    variance /= float64(len(mainChannels))
    
    // Synchronization = 1 - (variance / avgFlow) if avgFlow > 0
    if avgFlow == 0 {
        return 0.0
    }
    
    sync := 1.0 - (variance / avgFlow)
    if sync < 0 {
        sync = 0
    }
    if sync > 1 {
        sync = 1
    }
    
    return sync
}
```

### **áº¢nh HÆ°á»Ÿng Cá»§a Kinh Máº¡ch Äáº¿n Speed System**

#### **1. Combat Speed (Tá»‘c Äá»™ Chiáº¿n Äáº¥u)**
```go
// Calculate combat speed from meridians (ä»ç»è„‰è®¡ç®—æˆ˜æ–—é€Ÿåº¦) - TÃ­nh tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ chiáº¿n Ä‘áº¥u tá»« kinh máº¡ch
func CalculateCombatSpeed(meridians MeridianSystem) float64 {
    // Base combat speed (åŸºç¡€æˆ˜æ–—é€Ÿåº¦) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ chiáº¿n Ä‘áº¥u cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseSpeed := 1.0
    
    // Meridian flow rate affects reaction speed (ç»è„‰æµé€Ÿå½±å“ååº”é€Ÿåº¦) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ dÃ²ng cháº£y áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ pháº£n á»©ng
    flowFactor := meridians.MeridianCapacity.MaxFlowRate * 0.3
    
    // Channel synchronization affects coordination (é€šé“åŒæ­¥å½±å“åè°ƒæ€§) - Äá»“ng bá»™ kÃªnh áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng sá»± phá»‘i há»£p
    syncFactor := CalculateChannelSynchronization(meridians.MeridianChannels) * 0.4
    
    // Meridian efficiency affects energy utilization (ç»è„‰æ•ˆç‡å½±å“èƒ½é‡åˆ©ç”¨) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t kinh máº¡ch áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng sá»­ dá»¥ng nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
    efficiencyFactor := (meridians.MeridianQuality.Conductivity + meridians.MeridianQuality.Toughness) / 2.0 * 0.3
    
    return baseSpeed + flowFactor + syncFactor + efficiencyFactor
}

// Calculate spell casting speed (è®¡ç®—æ–½æ³•é€Ÿåº¦) - TÃ­nh tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ thi triá»ƒn phÃ¡p thuáº­t
func CalculateSpellCastingSpeed(meridians MeridianSystem, spiritSea SpiritSea) float64 {
    // Base casting speed (åŸºç¡€æ–½æ³•é€Ÿåº¦) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ thi triá»ƒn cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseSpeed := 1.0
    
    // Meridian conductivity affects qi flow to hands (ç»è„‰ä¼ å¯¼æ€§å½±å“æ°”åˆ°æ‰‹éƒ¨) - Äá»™ dáº«n kinh máº¡ch áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng dÃ²ng khÃ­ Ä‘áº¿n tay
    conductivityFactor := meridians.MeridianQuality.Conductivity * 0.4
    
    // Channel health affects stability (é€šé“å¥åº·å½±å“ç¨³å®šæ€§) - Sá»©c khá»e kÃªnh áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng Ä‘á»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh
    healthFactor := CalculateMainChannelHealth(meridians.MeridianChannels.MainChannels) * 0.3
    
    // Spirit sea control affects precision (è¯†æµ·æ§åˆ¶å½±å“ç²¾ç¡®åº¦) - Äiá»u khiá»ƒn thá»©c háº£i áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng Ä‘á»™ chÃ­nh xÃ¡c
    controlFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenControl * 0.3
    
    return baseSpeed + conductivityFactor + healthFactor + controlFactor
}

// Calculate movement speed (è®¡ç®—ç§»åŠ¨é€Ÿåº¦) - TÃ­nh tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ di chuyá»ƒn
func CalculateMovementSpeed(meridians MeridianSystem) float64 {
    // Base movement speed (åŸºç¡€ç§»åŠ¨é€Ÿåº¦) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ di chuyá»ƒn cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseSpeed := 1.0
    
    // Foot channel health affects leg strength (è¶³ç»å¥åº·å½±å“è…¿éƒ¨åŠ›é‡) - Sá»©c khá»e kÃªnh chÃ¢n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng sá»©c máº¡nh chÃ¢n
    footChannels := []MeridianChannel{
        meridians.MeridianChannels.MainChannels.FootTaiyinSpleen,
        meridians.MeridianChannels.MainChannels.FootYangmingStomach,
        meridians.MeridianChannels.MainChannels.FootShaoyinKidney,
        meridians.MeridianChannels.MainChannels.FootTaiyangBladder,
        meridians.MeridianChannels.MainChannels.FootJueyinLiver,
        meridians.MeridianChannels.MainChannels.FootShaoyangGallbladder,
    }
    
    footHealth := 0.0
    for _, channel := range footChannels {
        footHealth += channel.ChannelHealth
    }
    footHealth /= float64(len(footChannels))
    
    // Meridian flow efficiency affects energy distribution (ç»è„‰æµåŠ¨æ•ˆç‡å½±å“èƒ½é‡åˆ†é…) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t dÃ²ng cháº£y áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng phÃ¢n phá»‘i nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
    flowEfficiencyFactor := meridians.MeridianCapacity.FlowEfficiency * 0.5
    
    // Channel balance affects overall coordination (é€šé“å¹³è¡¡å½±å“æ•´ä½“åè°ƒ) - CÃ¢n báº±ng kÃªnh áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng sá»± phá»‘i há»£p tá»•ng thá»ƒ
    balanceFactor := CalculateChannelBalance(meridians.MeridianChannels) * 0.3
    
    return baseSpeed + footHealth*0.4 + flowEfficiencyFactor + balanceFactor
}
```

#### **2. Cultivation Speed (Tá»‘c Äá»™ Tu Luyá»‡n)**
```go
// Calculate cultivation speed from meridians (ä»ç»è„‰è®¡ç®—ä¿®ç‚¼é€Ÿåº¦) - TÃ­nh tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ tu luyá»‡n tá»« kinh máº¡ch
func CalculateCultivationSpeed(meridians MeridianSystem, dantian DantianInfo) float64 {
    // Base cultivation speed (åŸºç¡€ä¿®ç‚¼é€Ÿåº¦) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ tu luyá»‡n cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseSpeed := 1.0
    
    // Meridian conductivity affects qi absorption (ç»è„‰ä¼ å¯¼æ€§å½±å“æ°”å¸æ”¶) - Äá»™ dáº«n kinh máº¡ch áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng háº¥p thá»¥ khÃ­
    conductivityFactor := meridians.MeridianQuality.Conductivity * 0.3
    
    // Meridian capacity affects qi storage (ç»è„‰å®¹é‡å½±å“æ°”å­˜å‚¨) - Dung lÆ°á»£ng kinh máº¡ch áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng lÆ°u trá»¯ khÃ­
    capacityFactor := meridians.MeridianCapacity.TotalCapacity / 1000000.0 * 0.2 // Normalize to reasonable range
    
    // Channel health affects stability during cultivation (é€šé“å¥åº·å½±å“ä¿®ç‚¼ç¨³å®šæ€§) - Sá»©c khá»e kÃªnh áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng Ä‘á»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh khi tu luyá»‡n
    healthFactor := CalculateMainChannelHealth(meridians.MeridianChannels.MainChannels) * 0.2
    
    // Jing efficiency affects resource utilization (ç²¾æ•ˆç‡å½±å“èµ„æºåˆ©ç”¨) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t tinh áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng sá»­ dá»¥ng tÃ i nguyÃªn
    jingFactor := meridians.JingReserve.JingEfficiency * 0.2
    
    // Dantian purity affects conversion efficiency (ä¸¹ç”°çº¯åº¦å½±å“è½¬æ¢æ•ˆç‡) - Äá»™ tinh khiáº¿t Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng hiá»‡u suáº¥t chuyá»ƒn Ä‘á»•i
    dantianFactor := dantian.Quality.DantianPurity * 0.1
    
    return baseSpeed + conductivityFactor + capacityFactor + healthFactor + jingFactor + dantianFactor
}

// Calculate breakthrough speed (è®¡ç®—çªç ´é€Ÿåº¦) - TÃ­nh tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ Ä‘á»™t phÃ¡
func CalculateBreakthroughSpeed(meridians MeridianSystem, spiritSea SpiritSea) float64 {
    // Base breakthrough speed (åŸºç¡€çªç ´é€Ÿåº¦) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ Ä‘á»™t phÃ¡ cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseSpeed := 1.0
    
    // Meridian stability affects breakthrough success (ç»è„‰ç¨³å®šæ€§å½±å“çªç ´æˆåŠŸ) - Äá»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh kinh máº¡ch áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng thÃ nh cÃ´ng Ä‘á»™t phÃ¡
    stabilityFactor := meridians.MeridianCultivation.MeridianStability * 0.4
    
    // Channel synchronization affects energy coordination (é€šé“åŒæ­¥å½±å“èƒ½é‡åè°ƒ) - Äá»“ng bá»™ kÃªnh áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng phá»‘i há»£p nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
    syncFactor := CalculateChannelSynchronization(meridians.MeridianChannels) * 0.3
    
    // Spirit sea clarity affects focus (è¯†æµ·æ¸…æ™°åº¦å½±å“ä¸“æ³¨) - Äá»™ tinh tÆ°á»ng thá»©c háº£i áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng sá»± táº­p trung
    clarityFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenClarity * 0.3
    
    return baseSpeed + stabilityFactor + syncFactor + clarityFactor
}
```

#### **3. Derived Stats tá»« Kinh Máº¡ch**
```go
// Meridian-derived stats (ç»è„‰æ´¾ç”Ÿå±æ€§) - CÃ¡c derived stats tá»« kinh máº¡ch
var MeridianDerivedStats = []string{
    // Speed-related stats (é€Ÿåº¦ç›¸å…³å±æ€§) - Stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n tá»‘c Ä‘á»™
    "combat_speed",              // Combat speed (æˆ˜æ–—é€Ÿåº¦) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ chiáº¿n Ä‘áº¥u
    "spell_casting_speed",       // Spell casting speed (æ–½æ³•é€Ÿåº¦) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ thi triá»ƒn phÃ¡p thuáº­t
    "movement_speed",            // Movement speed (ç§»åŠ¨é€Ÿåº¦) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ di chuyá»ƒn
    "reaction_speed",            // Reaction speed (ååº”é€Ÿåº¦) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ pháº£n á»©ng
    "attack_speed",              // Attack speed (æ”»å‡»é€Ÿåº¦) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ táº¥n cÃ´ng
    
    // Cultivation-related stats (ä¿®ç‚¼ç›¸å…³å±æ€§) - Stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n tu luyá»‡n
    "cultivation_speed",         // Cultivation speed (ä¿®ç‚¼é€Ÿåº¦) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ tu luyá»‡n
    "breakthrough_speed",        // Breakthrough speed (çªç ´é€Ÿåº¦) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ Ä‘á»™t phÃ¡
    "qi_absorption_rate",        // Qi absorption rate (æ°”å¸æ”¶ç‡) - Tá»· lá»‡ háº¥p thá»¥ khÃ­
    "jing_consumption_rate",     // Jing consumption rate (ç²¾æ¶ˆè€—ç‡) - Tá»· lá»‡ tiÃªu hao tinh
    "energy_efficiency",         // Energy efficiency (èƒ½é‡æ•ˆç‡) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
    
    // Stability and control stats (ç¨³å®šæ€§å’Œæ§åˆ¶å±æ€§) - Stats á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh vÃ  Ä‘iá»u khiá»ƒn
    "meridian_stability",        // Meridian stability (ç»è„‰ç¨³å®šæ€§) - Äá»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh kinh máº¡ch
    "channel_balance",           // Channel balance (é€šé“å¹³è¡¡) - CÃ¢n báº±ng kÃªnh
    "flow_control",              // Flow control (æµåŠ¨æ§åˆ¶) - Äiá»u khiá»ƒn dÃ²ng cháº£y
    "pressure_tolerance",        // Pressure tolerance (å‹åŠ›è€å—) - Kháº£ nÄƒng chá»‹u Ã¡p lá»±c
    "recovery_speed",            // Recovery speed (æ¢å¤é€Ÿåº¦) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ phá»¥c há»“i
}

// Calculate meridian-derived stats (è®¡ç®—ç»è„‰æ´¾ç”Ÿå±æ€§) - TÃ­nh cÃ¡c derived stats tá»« kinh máº¡ch
func CalculateMeridianDerivedStats(meridians MeridianSystem, dantian DantianInfo, spiritSea SpiritSea) map[string]float64 {
    stats := make(map[string]float64)
    
    // Speed-related stats (é€Ÿåº¦ç›¸å…³å±æ€§) - Stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n tá»‘c Ä‘á»™
    stats["combat_speed"] = CalculateCombatSpeed(meridians)
    stats["spell_casting_speed"] = CalculateSpellCastingSpeed(meridians, spiritSea)
    stats["movement_speed"] = CalculateMovementSpeed(meridians)
    stats["reaction_speed"] = meridians.MeridianCapacity.MaxFlowRate * 0.8 + meridians.MeridianQuality.Conductivity * 0.2
    stats["attack_speed"] = CalculateCombatSpeed(meridians) * 0.9 // Slightly slower than combat speed
    
    // Cultivation-related stats (ä¿®ç‚¼ç›¸å…³å±æ€§) - Stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n tu luyá»‡n
    stats["cultivation_speed"] = CalculateCultivationSpeed(meridians, dantian)
    stats["breakthrough_speed"] = CalculateBreakthroughSpeed(meridians, spiritSea)
    stats["qi_absorption_rate"] = meridians.MeridianQuality.Conductivity * 0.6 + meridians.MeridianCapacity.FlowEfficiency * 0.4
    stats["jing_consumption_rate"] = meridians.JingReserve.JingConsumption
    stats["energy_efficiency"] = (meridians.MeridianQuality.Conductivity + meridians.MeridianQuality.Toughness) / 2.0
    
    // Stability and control stats (ç¨³å®šæ€§å’Œæ§åˆ¶å±æ€§) - Stats á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh vÃ  Ä‘iá»u khiá»ƒn
    stats["meridian_stability"] = meridians.MeridianCultivation.MeridianStability
    stats["channel_balance"] = CalculateChannelBalance(meridians.MeridianChannels)
    stats["flow_control"] = CalculateChannelSynchronization(meridians.MeridianChannels)
    stats["pressure_tolerance"] = meridians.MeridianCapacity.PressureTolerance
    stats["recovery_speed"] = meridians.MeridianQuality.Resilience * 0.7 + meridians.JingReserve.JingRegeneration * 0.3
    
    return stats
}
```

#### **4. áº¢nh HÆ°á»Ÿng Äáº¿n CÃ¡c Hoáº¡t Äá»™ng Cá»¥ Thá»ƒ**

**Combat System:**
```go
// Calculate attack cooldown (è®¡ç®—æ”»å‡»å†·å´) - TÃ­nh thá»i gian há»“i chiÃªu táº¥n cÃ´ng
func CalculateAttackCooldown(meridians MeridianSystem) float64 {
    baseCooldown := 2.0 // 2 seconds base cooldown
    speedFactor := CalculateCombatSpeed(meridians)
    return baseCooldown / speedFactor
}

// Calculate spell cooldown (è®¡ç®—æ³•æœ¯å†·å´) - TÃ­nh thá»i gian há»“i chiÃªu phÃ¡p thuáº­t
func CalculateSpellCooldown(meridians MeridianSystem, spiritSea SpiritSea) float64 {
    baseCooldown := 3.0 // 3 seconds base cooldown
    speedFactor := CalculateSpellCastingSpeed(meridians, spiritSea)
    return baseCooldown / speedFactor
}
```

**Cultivation System:**
```go
// Calculate cultivation time (è®¡ç®—ä¿®ç‚¼æ—¶é—´) - TÃ­nh thá»i gian tu luyá»‡n
func CalculateCultivationTime(meridians MeridianSystem, dantian DantianInfo, targetExp float64) float64 {
    baseTime := targetExp / 1000.0 // Base time in hours
    speedFactor := CalculateCultivationSpeed(meridians, dantian)
    return baseTime / speedFactor
}

// Calculate breakthrough time (è®¡ç®—çªç ´æ—¶é—´) - TÃ­nh thá»i gian Ä‘á»™t phÃ¡
func CalculateBreakthroughTime(meridians MeridianSystem, spiritSea SpiritSea, realmLevel int64) float64 {
    baseTime := float64(realmLevel) * 24.0 // Base time in hours (24h per realm level)
    speedFactor := CalculateBreakthroughSpeed(meridians, spiritSea)
    return baseTime / speedFactor
}
```

### **áº¢nh HÆ°á»Ÿng Cá»§a Äan Äiá»n Äáº¿n Energy System (Há»‡ Thá»‘ng NÄƒng LÆ°á»£ng)**

// Energy types in Jindan System (é‡‘ä¸¹ç³»ç»Ÿä¸­çš„èƒ½é‡ç±»å‹) - CÃ¡c loáº¡i nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng trong há»‡ thá»‘ng kim Ä‘an

    // Special energies (ç‰¹æ®Šèƒ½é‡) - NÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng Ä‘áº·c biá»‡t

    EnergyTypeTuVi      EnergyType = "tu_vi"      // Tu Vi (ä¿®ä¸º) - Tu vi

// Energy configuration (èƒ½é‡é…ç½®) - Cáº¥u hÃ¬nh nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
type EnergyConfig struct {
    Type        EnergyType `json:"type"`         // Energy type (èƒ½é‡ç±»å‹) - Loáº¡i nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
    Name        string     `json:"name"`         // Display name (æ˜¾ç¤ºåç§°) - TÃªn hiá»ƒn thá»‹
    Description string     `json:"description"`  // Description (æè¿°) - MÃ´ táº£
    BaseValue   float64    `json:"base_value"`   // Base value (åŸºç¡€å€¼) - GiÃ¡ trá»‹ cÆ¡ báº£n
    MaxValue    float64    `json:"max_value"`    // Max value (æœ€å¤§å€¼) - GiÃ¡ trá»‹ tá»‘i Ä‘a
    RegenRate   float64    `json:"regen_rate"`   // Regeneration rate (æ¢å¤ç‡) - Tá»· lá»‡ há»“i phá»¥c
    DecayRate   float64    `json:"decay_rate"`   // Decay rate (è¡°å‡ç‡) - Tá»· lá»‡ suy giáº£m
}

// Get all energy types (è·å–æ‰€æœ‰èƒ½é‡ç±»å‹) - Láº¥y táº¥t cáº£ loáº¡i nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng

    return []EnergyType{
