#### **2. Energy Calculation from Dantian (TÃ­nh NÄƒng LÆ°á»£ng tá»« Äan Äiá»n)**
```go
// Calculate energy from dantian (ä»ä¸¹ç”°è®¡ç®—èƒ½é‡) - TÃ­nh nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng tá»« Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
func CalculateEnergyFromDantian(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem, energyType EnergyType) float64 {
    config := GetEnergyConfigs()[energyType]
    
    // Base value from config (ä»é…ç½®è·å–åŸºç¡€å€¼) - Láº¥y giÃ¡ trá»‹ cÆ¡ báº£n tá»« cáº¥u hÃ¬nh
    baseValue := config.BaseValue
    
    // Dantian capacity affects all energies (ä¸¹ç”°å®¹é‡å½±å“æ‰€æœ‰èƒ½é‡) - Dung lÆ°á»£ng Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng táº¥t cáº£ nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
    capacityFactor := dantian.Storage.DantianCapacity / 1000.0
    
    // Dantian purity affects energy quality (ä¸¹ç”°çº¯åº¦å½±å“èƒ½é‡è´¨é‡) - Äá»™ tinh khiáº¿t Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng cháº¥t lÆ°á»£ng nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
    purityFactor := dantian.Quality.DantianPurity
    
    // Dantian level affects energy strength (ä¸¹ç”°ç­‰çº§å½±å“èƒ½é‡å¼ºåº¦) - Cáº¥p Ä‘á»™ Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng sá»©c máº¡nh nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
    levelFactor := float64(dantian.Core.DantianLevel)
    
    // Meridian health affects energy flow (ç»è„‰å¥åº·å½±å“èƒ½é‡æµåŠ¨) - Sá»©c khá»e kinh máº¡ch áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng dÃ²ng cháº£y nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
    meridianHealth := CalculateMainChannelHealth(meridians.MeridianChannels.MainChannels)
    
    // Calculate energy based on type (æ ¹æ®ç±»å‹è®¡ç®—èƒ½é‡) - TÃ­nh nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng dá»±a trÃªn loáº¡i
    switch energyType {
    case EnergyTypeHP:
        return baseValue + capacityFactor*0.4 + purityFactor*50.0*0.3 + levelFactor*20.0*0.2 + meridianHealth*30.0*0.1
    case EnergyTypeStamina:
        return baseValue + capacityFactor*0.3 + purityFactor*40.0*0.4 + levelFactor*15.0*0.3
    case EnergyTypeMana:
        return baseValue + capacityFactor*0.5 + purityFactor*80.0*0.3 + levelFactor*30.0*0.2
    case EnergyTypeQi:
        return baseValue + capacityFactor*0.6 + purityFactor*100.0*0.4 + levelFactor*50.0*0.3 + meridianHealth*20.0*0.2
    case EnergyTypeLingQi:
        return baseValue + capacityFactor*0.7 + purityFactor*150.0*0.5 + levelFactor*80.0*0.4 + meridianHealth*25.0*0.3
    case EnergyTypeXianQi:
        return baseValue + capacityFactor*0.8 + purityFactor*200.0*0.6 + levelFactor*120.0*0.5 + meridianHealth*30.0*0.4
    case EnergyTypeShenQi:
        return baseValue + capacityFactor*0.9 + purityFactor*300.0*0.7 + levelFactor*200.0*0.6 + meridianHealth*40.0*0.5
    case EnergyTypeJing:
        return baseValue + capacityFactor*0.2 + purityFactor*30.0*0.3 + levelFactor*10.0*0.2
    case EnergyTypeShen:
        return baseValue + capacityFactor*0.3 + purityFactor*40.0*0.4 + levelFactor*15.0*0.3
    case EnergyTypeTuVi:
        // Tu Vi is calculated differently (Tu Vi Ä‘Æ°á»£c tÃ­nh khÃ¡c) - Tu Vi Ä‘Æ°á»£c tÃ­nh tá»« power level
        return CalculateTuViFromPowerLevel(dantian.Core.PowerLevel)
    case EnergyTypeYuanLi:
        return baseValue + capacityFactor*0.4 + purityFactor*60.0*0.5 + levelFactor*25.0*0.4 + meridianHealth*15.0*0.3
    case EnergyTypeNianLi:
        // Nian Li is calculated from Spirit Sea, not Dantian (Niá»‡m lá»±c Ä‘Æ°á»£c tÃ­nh tá»« thá»©c háº£i, khÃ´ng pháº£i Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n) - Nian Li is calculated from Spirit Sea
        return 0.0 // Will be calculated separately in Spirit Sea section
    default:
        return baseValue
    }
}

// Calculate energy regeneration from dantian (ä»ä¸¹ç”°è®¡ç®—èƒ½é‡æ¢å¤) - TÃ­nh há»“i phá»¥c nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng tá»« Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
func CalculateEnergyRegeneration(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem, energyType EnergyType) float64 {
    config := GetEnergyConfigs()[energyType]
    
    // Base regen rate from config (ä»é…ç½®è·å–åŸºç¡€æ¢å¤ç‡) - Láº¥y tá»· lá»‡ há»“i phá»¥c cÆ¡ báº£n tá»« cáº¥u hÃ¬nh
    baseRegen := config.RegenRate
    
    // Dantian efficiency affects regeneration (ä¸¹ç”°æ•ˆç‡å½±å“æ¢å¤) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng há»“i phá»¥c
    efficiencyFactor := dantian.Quality.DantianEfficiency
    
    // Dantian stability affects consistent regen (ä¸¹ç”°ç¨³å®šæ€§å½±å“æŒç»­æ¢å¤) - Äá»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng há»“i phá»¥c liÃªn tá»¥c
    stabilityFactor := dantian.Quality.DantianStability
    
    // Meridian flow affects energy circulation (ç»è„‰æµåŠ¨å½±å“èƒ½é‡å¾ªç¯) - DÃ²ng cháº£y kinh máº¡ch áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng tuáº§n hoÃ n nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
    flowFactor := meridians.MeridianCapacity.FlowEfficiency
    
    // Calculate regen based on type (æ ¹æ®ç±»å‹è®¡ç®—æ¢å¤) - TÃ­nh há»“i phá»¥c dá»±a trÃªn loáº¡i
    switch energyType {
    case EnergyTypeHP:
        return baseRegen + efficiencyFactor*0.5 + stabilityFactor*0.3 + flowFactor*0.2
    case EnergyTypeStamina:
        return baseRegen + efficiencyFactor*0.6 + stabilityFactor*0.4 + flowFactor*0.3
    case EnergyTypeMana:
        return baseRegen + efficiencyFactor*0.7 + stabilityFactor*0.4 + flowFactor*0.2
    case EnergyTypeQi:
        return baseRegen + efficiencyFactor*0.8 + stabilityFactor*0.5 + flowFactor*0.4
    case EnergyTypeLingQi:
        return baseRegen + efficiencyFactor*0.9 + stabilityFactor*0.6 + flowFactor*0.5
    case EnergyTypeXianQi:
        return baseRegen + efficiencyFactor*1.0 + stabilityFactor*0.7 + flowFactor*0.6
    case EnergyTypeShenQi:
        return baseRegen + efficiencyFactor*1.1 + stabilityFactor*0.8 + flowFactor*0.7
    case EnergyTypeJing:
        return baseRegen + efficiencyFactor*0.3 + stabilityFactor*0.2 + flowFactor*0.1
    case EnergyTypeShen:
        return baseRegen + efficiencyFactor*0.4 + stabilityFactor*0.3 + flowFactor*0.2
    case EnergyTypeTuVi:
        return 0.0 // Tu Vi doesn't regenerate naturally
    case EnergyTypeYuanLi:
        return baseRegen + efficiencyFactor*0.5 + stabilityFactor*0.4 + flowFactor*0.3
    case EnergyTypeNianLi:
        return 0.0 // Nian Li regeneration is calculated from Spirit Sea
    default:
        return baseRegen
    }
}

// Calculate energy cap from dantian (ä»ä¸¹ç”°è®¡ç®—èƒ½é‡ä¸Šé™) - TÃ­nh giá»›i háº¡n nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng tá»« Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
func CalculateEnergyCap(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem, energyType EnergyType) float64 {
    config := GetEnergyConfigs()[energyType]
    
    // Base cap from config (ä»é…ç½®è·å–åŸºç¡€ä¸Šé™) - Láº¥y giá»›i háº¡n cÆ¡ báº£n tá»« cáº¥u hÃ¬nh
    baseCap := config.MaxValue
    
    // Dantian capacity directly affects energy cap (ä¸¹ç”°å®¹é‡ç›´æ¥å½±å“èƒ½é‡ä¸Šé™) - Dung lÆ°á»£ng Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng trá»±c tiáº¿p giá»›i háº¡n nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
    capacityFactor := dantian.Storage.DantianCapacity / 100.0
    
    // Dantian quality affects energy quality (ä¸¹ç”°è´¨é‡å½±å“èƒ½é‡è´¨é‡) - Cháº¥t lÆ°á»£ng Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng cháº¥t lÆ°á»£ng nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
    qualityFactor := (dantian.Quality.DantianPurity + dantian.Quality.DantianEfficiency) / 2.0
    
    // Meridian capacity affects energy storage (ç»è„‰å®¹é‡å½±å“èƒ½é‡å­˜å‚¨) - Dung lÆ°á»£ng kinh máº¡ch áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng lÆ°u trá»¯ nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
    meridianFactor := meridians.MeridianCapacity.TotalCapacity / 10000.0
    
    // Calculate cap based on type (æ ¹æ®ç±»å‹è®¡ç®—ä¸Šé™) - TÃ­nh giá»›i háº¡n dá»±a trÃªn loáº¡i
    switch energyType {
    case EnergyTypeHP:
        return baseCap + capacityFactor*0.6 + qualityFactor*100.0*0.3 + meridianFactor*0.1
    case EnergyTypeStamina:
        return baseCap + capacityFactor*0.5 + qualityFactor*80.0*0.4 + meridianFactor*0.1
    case EnergyTypeMana:
        return baseCap + capacityFactor*0.7 + qualityFactor*150.0*0.2 + meridianFactor*0.1
    case EnergyTypeQi:
        return baseCap + capacityFactor*0.8 + qualityFactor*200.0*0.3 + meridianFactor*0.2
    case EnergyTypeLingQi:
        return baseCap + capacityFactor*0.9 + qualityFactor*300.0*0.4 + meridianFactor*0.3
    case EnergyTypeXianQi:
        return baseCap + capacityFactor*1.0 + qualityFactor*500.0*0.5 + meridianFactor*0.4
    case EnergyTypeShenQi:
        return baseCap + capacityFactor*1.1 + qualityFactor*800.0*0.6 + meridianFactor*0.5
    case EnergyTypeJing:
        return baseCap + capacityFactor*0.3 + qualityFactor*50.0*0.2 + meridianFactor*0.05
    case EnergyTypeShen:
        return baseCap + capacityFactor*0.4 + qualityFactor*60.0*0.3 + meridianFactor*0.05
    case EnergyTypeTuVi:
        return baseCap // Tu Vi cap is based on power level, not dantian
    case EnergyTypeYuanLi:
        return baseCap + capacityFactor*0.6 + qualityFactor*120.0*0.4 + meridianFactor*0.2
    case EnergyTypeNianLi:
        return baseCap // Nian Li cap is calculated from Spirit Sea
    default:
        return baseCap
    }
}
```

#### **3. Integration with Actor Core v3 (TÃ­ch Há»£p vá»›i Actor Core v3)**
```go
// Convert Jindan System to Actor Core v3 SubsystemOutput (è½¬æ¢é‡‘ä¸¹ç³»ç»Ÿåˆ°Actor Core v3 SubsystemOutput) - Chuyá»ƒn Ä‘á»•i há»‡ thá»‘ng kim Ä‘an sang SubsystemOutput cá»§a Actor Core v3
func ConvertToSubsystemOutput(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem, spiritSea SpiritSea) *interfaces.SubsystemOutput {
    // Calculate all energies (è®¡ç®—æ‰€æœ‰èƒ½é‡) - TÃ­nh táº¥t cáº£ nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
    energyValues := make(map[EnergyType]float64)
    energyRegens := make(map[EnergyType]float64)
    energyCaps := make(map[EnergyType]float64)
    
    for _, energyType := range GetAllEnergyTypes() {
        energyValues[energyType] = CalculateEnergyFromDantian(dantian, meridians, energyType)
        energyRegens[energyType] = CalculateEnergyRegeneration(dantian, meridians, energyType)
        energyCaps[energyType] = CalculateEnergyCap(dantian, meridians, energyType)
    }
    
    // Create primary contributions (åˆ›å»ºä¸»è¦è´¡çŒ®) - Táº¡o cÃ¡c Ä‘Ã³ng gÃ³p chÃ­nh
    primaryContributions := make([]interfaces.Contribution, 0)
    
    // Add dantian primary stats (æ·»åŠ ä¸¹ç”°ä¸»è¦å±æ€§) - ThÃªm cÃ¡c primary stats cá»§a Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
    dantianPrimaryStats := CalculateDantianPrimaryStats(dantian, meridians)
    for statName, value := range dantianPrimaryStats {
        primaryContributions = append(primaryContributions, interfaces.Contribution{
            Dimension: statName,
            Bucket:    "dantian",
            Value:     value,
            System:    "jindan_system",
            Priority:  100,
        })
    }
    
    // Add meridian primary stats (æ·»åŠ ç»è„‰ä¸»è¦å±æ€§) - ThÃªm cÃ¡c primary stats cá»§a kinh máº¡ch
    meridianPrimaryStats := CalculateMeridianPrimaryStats(meridians)
    for statName, value := range meridianPrimaryStats {
        primaryContributions = append(primaryContributions, interfaces.Contribution{
            Dimension: statName,
            Bucket:    "meridians",
            Value:     value,
            System:    "jindan_system",
            Priority:  90,
        })
    }
    
    // Add spirit sea primary stats (æ·»åŠ è¯†æµ·ä¸»è¦å±æ€§) - ThÃªm cÃ¡c primary stats cá»§a thá»©c háº£i
    spiritSeaPrimaryStats := CalculateSpiritSeaPrimaryStats(spiritSea)
    for statName, value := range spiritSeaPrimaryStats {
        primaryContributions = append(primaryContributions, interfaces.Contribution{
            Dimension: statName,
            Bucket:    "spirit_sea",
            Value:     value,
            System:    "jindan_system",
            Priority:  80,
        })
    }
    
    // Create derived contributions (åˆ›å»ºæ´¾ç”Ÿè´¡çŒ®) - Táº¡o cÃ¡c Ä‘Ã³ng gÃ³p dáº«n xuáº¥t
    derivedContributions := make([]interfaces.Contribution, 0)
    
    // Add energy values as derived stats (æ·»åŠ èƒ½é‡å€¼ä½œä¸ºæ´¾ç”Ÿå±æ€§) - ThÃªm giÃ¡ trá»‹ nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng nhÆ° derived stats
    for energyType, value := range energyValues {
        derivedContributions = append(derivedContributions, interfaces.Contribution{
            Dimension: string(energyType),
            Bucket:    "energy",
            Value:     value,
            System:    "jindan_system",
            Priority:  100,
        })
    }
    
    // Add energy regeneration rates (æ·»åŠ èƒ½é‡æ¢å¤ç‡) - ThÃªm tá»· lá»‡ há»“i phá»¥c nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
    for energyType, regen := range energyRegens {
        derivedContributions = append(derivedContributions, interfaces.Contribution{
            Dimension: string(energyType) + "_regen",
            Bucket:    "energy_regen",
            Value:     regen,
            System:    "jindan_system",
            Priority:  90,
        })
    }
    
    // Add energy caps (æ·»åŠ èƒ½é‡ä¸Šé™) - ThÃªm giá»›i háº¡n nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
    for energyType, cap := range energyCaps {
        derivedContributions = append(derivedContributions, interfaces.Contribution{
            Dimension: string(energyType) + "_cap",
            Bucket:    "energy_cap",
            Value:     cap,
            System:    "jindan_system",
            Priority:  80,
        })
    }
    
    // Add speed-related derived stats (æ·»åŠ é€Ÿåº¦ç›¸å…³æ´¾ç”Ÿå±æ€§) - ThÃªm cÃ¡c derived stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n tá»‘c Ä‘á»™
    speedStats := CalculateMeridianDerivedStats(meridians, dantian, spiritSea)
    for statName, value := range speedStats {
        derivedContributions = append(derivedContributions, interfaces.Contribution{
            Dimension: statName,
            Bucket:    "speed",
            Value:     value,
            System:    "jindan_system",
            Priority:  70,
        })
    }
    
    // Create cap contributions (åˆ›å»ºä¸Šé™è´¡çŒ®) - Táº¡o cÃ¡c Ä‘Ã³ng gÃ³p giá»›i háº¡n
    capContributions := make([]interfaces.CapContribution, 0)
    
    // Add energy caps (æ·»åŠ èƒ½é‡ä¸Šé™) - ThÃªm giá»›i háº¡n nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
    for energyType, cap := range energyCaps {
        capContributions = append(capContributions, interfaces.CapContribution{
            System:    "jindan_system",
            Dimension: string(energyType),
            Mode:      "HARD_MAX",
            Kind:      "ENERGY",
            Value:     cap,
            Priority:  100,
            Scope:     "REALM",
            Realm:     GetCurrentRealm(dantian.Core.DantianLevel),
            Tags:      []string{"energy", "dantian"},
        })
    }
    
    // Create context modifiers (åˆ›å»ºä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡ä¿®é¥°ç¬¦) - Táº¡o cÃ¡c bá»™ Ä‘iá»u chá»‰nh ngá»¯ cáº£nh
    contextModifiers := make(map[string]interfaces.ModifierPack)
    
    // Add dantian quality modifiers (æ·»åŠ ä¸¹ç”°è´¨é‡ä¿®é¥°ç¬¦) - ThÃªm bá»™ Ä‘iá»u chá»‰nh cháº¥t lÆ°á»£ng Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
    contextModifiers["dantian_quality"] = interfaces.ModifierPack{
        AdditivePercent: dantian.Quality.DantianPurity * 0.1,
        Multipliers:     []float64{dantian.Quality.DantianEfficiency},
        PostAdd:         dantian.Quality.DantianStability * 0.05,
    }
    
    // Add meridian flow modifiers (æ·»åŠ ç»è„‰æµåŠ¨ä¿®é¥°ç¬¦) - ThÃªm bá»™ Ä‘iá»u chá»‰nh dÃ²ng cháº£y kinh máº¡ch
    contextModifiers["meridian_flow"] = interfaces.ModifierPack{
        AdditivePercent: meridians.MeridianCapacity.FlowEfficiency * 0.2,
        Multipliers:     []float64{meridians.MeridianQuality.Conductivity},
        PostAdd:         meridians.MeridianQuality.Toughness * 0.1,
    }
    
    // Create subsystem metadata (åˆ›å»ºå­ç³»ç»Ÿå…ƒæ•°æ®) - Táº¡o siÃªu dá»¯ liá»‡u há»‡ thá»‘ng con
    meta := interfaces.SubsystemMeta{
        System:     "jindan_system",
        Version:    1,
        APILevel:   3,
        Compatible: true,
    }
    
    return &interfaces.SubsystemOutput{
        Primary: primaryContributions,
        Derived: derivedContributions,
        Caps:    capContributions,
        Context: contextModifiers,
        Meta:    meta,
    }
}
```

#### **4. Energy Management Functions (HÃ m Quáº£n LÃ½ NÄƒng LÆ°á»£ng)**
```go
// Energy management functions (èƒ½é‡ç®¡ç†å‡½æ•°) - CÃ¡c hÃ m quáº£n lÃ½ nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
type EnergyManager struct {
    dantian   DantianInfo
    meridians MeridianSystem
    spiritSea SpiritSea
}

// NewEnergyManager creates a new energy manager (åˆ›å»ºæ–°çš„èƒ½é‡ç®¡ç†å™¨) - Táº¡o energy manager má»›i
func NewEnergyManager(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem, spiritSea SpiritSea) *EnergyManager {
    return &EnergyManager{
        dantian:   dantian,
        meridians: meridians,
        spiritSea: spiritSea,
    }
}

// GetEnergyValue gets current energy value (è·å–å½“å‰èƒ½é‡å€¼) - Láº¥y giÃ¡ trá»‹ nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng hiá»‡n táº¡i
func (em *EnergyManager) GetEnergyValue(energyType EnergyType) float64 {
    return CalculateEnergyFromDantian(em.dantian, em.meridians, energyType)
}

// GetEnergyRegen gets energy regeneration rate (è·å–èƒ½é‡æ¢å¤ç‡) - Láº¥y tá»· lá»‡ há»“i phá»¥c nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
func (em *EnergyManager) GetEnergyRegen(energyType EnergyType) float64 {
    return CalculateEnergyRegeneration(em.dantian, em.meridians, energyType)
}

// GetEnergyCap gets energy capacity (è·å–èƒ½é‡å®¹é‡) - Láº¥y dung lÆ°á»£ng nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
func (em *EnergyManager) GetEnergyCap(energyType EnergyType) float64 {
    return CalculateEnergyCap(em.dantian, em.meridians, energyType)
}

// ConsumeEnergy consumes energy (æ¶ˆè€—èƒ½é‡) - TiÃªu hao nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
func (em *EnergyManager) ConsumeEnergy(energyType EnergyType, amount float64) bool {
    currentValue := em.GetEnergyValue(energyType)
    if currentValue < amount {
        return false // Not enough energy
    }
    
    // Update dantian storage (æ›´æ–°ä¸¹ç”°å­˜å‚¨) - Cáº­p nháº­t lÆ°u trá»¯ Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
    em.dantian.Storage.CurrentQi -= amount * 0.1 // Convert to Qi consumption
    return true
}

// RestoreEnergy restores energy (æ¢å¤èƒ½é‡) - Há»“i phá»¥c nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng
func (em *EnergyManager) RestoreEnergy(energyType EnergyType, amount float64) {
    regenRate := em.GetEnergyRegen(energyType)
    cap := em.GetEnergyCap(energyType)
    
    // Calculate restoration amount (è®¡ç®—æ¢å¤é‡) - TÃ­nh lÆ°á»£ng há»“i phá»¥c
    restoration := regenRate * amount
    if restoration > cap {
        restoration = cap
    }
    
    // Update dantian storage (æ›´æ–°ä¸¹ç”°å­˜å‚¨) - Cáº­p nháº­t lÆ°u trá»¯ Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
    em.dantian.Storage.CurrentQi += restoration * 0.1 // Convert to Qi restoration
}
```

#### **5. Combat Integration (TÃ­ch Há»£p Combat)**
```go
// Combat energy functions (æˆ˜æ–—èƒ½é‡å‡½æ•°) - CÃ¡c hÃ m nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng chiáº¿n Ä‘áº¥u
func (em *EnergyManager) CanCastSpell(spellCost map[EnergyType]float64) bool {
    for energyType, cost := range spellCost {
        if em.GetEnergyValue(energyType) < cost {
            return false
        }
    }
    return true
}

func (em *EnergyManager) CastSpell(spellCost map[EnergyType]float64) bool {
    if !em.CanCastSpell(spellCost) {
        return false
    }
    
    for energyType, cost := range spellCost {
        em.ConsumeEnergy(energyType, cost)
    }
    return true
}

func (em *EnergyManager) CanPerformAction(actionCost map[EnergyType]float64) bool {
    for energyType, cost := range actionCost {
        if em.GetEnergyValue(energyType) < cost {
            return false
        }
    }
    return true
}

func (em *EnergyManager) PerformAction(actionCost map[EnergyType]float64) bool {
    if !em.CanPerformAction(actionCost) {
        return false
    }
    
    for energyType, cost := range actionCost {
        em.ConsumeEnergy(energyType, cost)
    }
    return true
}
```

### **áº¢nh HÆ°á»Ÿng Cá»§a Äan Äiá»n Äáº¿n HP vÃ  MP**

#### **1. HP (Sinh Má»‡nh) - Health Points**
```go
// Calculate HP from dantian (ä»ä¸¹ç”°è®¡ç®—ç”Ÿå‘½å€¼) - TÃ­nh HP tá»« Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
func CalculateHPFromDantian(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem) float64 {
    // Base HP (åŸºç¡€ç”Ÿå‘½å€¼) - HP cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseHP := 100.0
    
    // Dantian capacity affects total life force (ä¸¹ç”°å®¹é‡å½±å“æ€»ç”Ÿå‘½åŠ›) - Dung lÆ°á»£ng Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng tá»•ng sinh lá»±c
    capacityFactor := dantian.Storage.DantianCapacity / 1000.0 * 0.4
    
    // Dantian purity affects life quality (ä¸¹ç”°çº¯åº¦å½±å“ç”Ÿå‘½è´¨é‡) - Äá»™ tinh khiáº¿t Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng cháº¥t lÆ°á»£ng sinh má»‡nh
    purityFactor := dantian.Quality.DantianPurity * 50.0 * 0.3
    
    // Dantian level affects life force strength (ä¸¹ç”°ç­‰çº§å½±å“ç”Ÿå‘½åŠ›å¼ºåº¦) - Cáº¥p Ä‘á»™ Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng sá»©c máº¡nh sinh lá»±c
    levelFactor := float64(dantian.Core.DantianLevel) * 20.0 * 0.2
    
    // Meridian health affects life circulation (ç»è„‰å¥åº·å½±å“ç”Ÿå‘½å¾ªç¯) - Sá»©c khá»e kinh máº¡ch áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng tuáº§n hoÃ n sinh má»‡nh
    meridianHealth := CalculateMainChannelHealth(meridians.MeridianChannels.MainChannels)
    meridianFactor := meridianHealth * 30.0 * 0.1
    
    return baseHP + capacityFactor + purityFactor + levelFactor + meridianFactor
}

// Calculate HP regeneration from dantian (ä»ä¸¹ç”°è®¡ç®—ç”Ÿå‘½æ¢å¤) - TÃ­nh há»“i phá»¥c HP tá»« Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
func CalculateHPRegeneration(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem) float64 {
    // Base HP regen (åŸºç¡€ç”Ÿå‘½æ¢å¤) - Há»“i phá»¥c HP cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseRegen := 1.0
    
    // Dantian efficiency affects life force regeneration (ä¸¹ç”°æ•ˆç‡å½±å“ç”Ÿå‘½åŠ›æ¢å¤) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng há»“i phá»¥c sinh lá»±c
    efficiencyFactor := dantian.Quality.DantianEfficiency * 0.5
    
    // Dantian stability affects consistent regeneration (ä¸¹ç”°ç¨³å®šæ€§å½±å“æŒç»­æ¢å¤) - Äá»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng há»“i phá»¥c liÃªn tá»¥c
    stabilityFactor := dantian.Quality.DantianStability * 0.3
    
    // Meridian flow affects life force circulation (ç»è„‰æµåŠ¨å½±å“ç”Ÿå‘½åŠ›å¾ªç¯) - DÃ²ng cháº£y kinh máº¡ch áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng tuáº§n hoÃ n sinh lá»±c
    flowFactor := meridians.MeridianCapacity.FlowEfficiency * 0.2
    
    return baseRegen + efficiencyFactor + stabilityFactor + flowFactor
}

// Calculate HP cap from dantian (ä»ä¸¹ç”°è®¡ç®—ç”Ÿå‘½ä¸Šé™) - TÃ­nh giá»›i háº¡n HP tá»« Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
func CalculateHPCap(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem) float64 {
    // Base HP cap (åŸºç¡€ç”Ÿå‘½ä¸Šé™) - Giá»›i háº¡n HP cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseCap := 1000.0
    
    // Dantian capacity directly affects HP cap (ä¸¹ç”°å®¹é‡ç›´æ¥å½±å“ç”Ÿå‘½ä¸Šé™) - Dung lÆ°á»£ng Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng trá»±c tiáº¿p giá»›i háº¡n HP
    capacityFactor := dantian.Storage.DantianCapacity / 100.0 * 0.6
    
    // Dantian quality affects HP quality (ä¸¹ç”°è´¨é‡å½±å“ç”Ÿå‘½è´¨é‡) - Cháº¥t lÆ°á»£ng Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng cháº¥t lÆ°á»£ng HP
    qualityFactor := (dantian.Quality.DantianPurity + dantian.Quality.DantianEfficiency) / 2.0 * 100.0 * 0.3
    
    // Meridian capacity affects life force storage (ç»è„‰å®¹é‡å½±å“ç”Ÿå‘½åŠ›å­˜å‚¨) - Dung lÆ°á»£ng kinh máº¡ch áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng lÆ°u trá»¯ sinh lá»±c
    meridianFactor := meridians.MeridianCapacity.TotalCapacity / 10000.0 * 0.1
    
    return baseCap + capacityFactor + qualityFactor + meridianFactor
}
```

#### **2. MP (Tu Vi/Linh KhÃ­/TiÃªn KhÃ­) - Mana Points**
```go
// Calculate MP from dantian (ä»ä¸¹ç”°è®¡ç®—æ³•åŠ›å€¼) - TÃ­nh MP tá»« Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
func CalculateMPFromDantian(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem) float64 {
    // Base MP (åŸºç¡€æ³•åŠ›å€¼) - MP cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseMP := 100.0
    
    // Dantian capacity directly affects MP (ä¸¹ç”°å®¹é‡ç›´æ¥å½±å“æ³•åŠ›å€¼) - Dung lÆ°á»£ng Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng trá»±c tiáº¿p MP
    capacityFactor := dantian.Storage.DantianCapacity / 1000.0 * 0.5
    
    // Dantian purity affects MP quality (ä¸¹ç”°çº¯åº¦å½±å“æ³•åŠ›è´¨é‡) - Äá»™ tinh khiáº¿t Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng cháº¥t lÆ°á»£ng MP
    purityFactor := dantian.Quality.DantianPurity * 80.0 * 0.3
    
    // Dantian level affects MP strength (ä¸¹ç”°ç­‰çº§å½±å“æ³•åŠ›å¼ºåº¦) - Cáº¥p Ä‘á»™ Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng sá»©c máº¡nh MP
    levelFactor := float64(dantian.Core.DantianLevel) * 30.0 * 0.2
    
    return baseMP + capacityFactor + purityFactor + levelFactor
}

// Calculate MP regeneration from dantian (ä»ä¸¹ç”°è®¡ç®—æ³•åŠ›æ¢å¤) - TÃ­nh há»“i phá»¥c MP tá»« Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
func CalculateMPRegeneration(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem) float64 {
    // Base MP regen (åŸºç¡€æ³•åŠ›æ¢å¤) - Há»“i phá»¥c MP cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseRegen := 2.0
    
    // Dantian efficiency affects MP regeneration (ä¸¹ç”°æ•ˆç‡å½±å“æ³•åŠ›æ¢å¤) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng há»“i phá»¥c MP
    efficiencyFactor := dantian.Quality.DantianEfficiency * 0.6
    
    // Dantian stability affects consistent MP regen (ä¸¹ç”°ç¨³å®šæ€§å½±å“æŒç»­æ³•åŠ›æ¢å¤) - Äá»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng há»“i phá»¥c MP liÃªn tá»¥c
    stabilityFactor := dantian.Quality.DantianStability * 0.4
    
    // Meridian conductivity affects qi flow to dantian (ç»è„‰ä¼ å¯¼æ€§å½±å“æ°”åˆ°ä¸¹ç”°) - Äá»™ dáº«n kinh máº¡ch áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng dÃ²ng khÃ­ Ä‘áº¿n Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
    conductivityFactor := meridians.MeridianQuality.Conductivity * 0.3
    
    // Meridian flow efficiency affects MP conversion (ç»è„‰æµåŠ¨æ•ˆç‡å½±å“æ³•åŠ›è½¬æ¢) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t dÃ²ng cháº£y kinh máº¡ch áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng chuyá»ƒn Ä‘á»•i MP
    flowFactor := meridians.MeridianCapacity.FlowEfficiency * 0.2
    
    return baseRegen + efficiencyFactor + stabilityFactor + conductivityFactor + flowFactor
}

// Calculate MP cap from dantian (ä»ä¸¹ç”°è®¡ç®—æ³•åŠ›ä¸Šé™) - TÃ­nh giá»›i háº¡n MP tá»« Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
func CalculateMPCap(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem) float64 {
    // Base MP cap (åŸºç¡€æ³•åŠ›ä¸Šé™) - Giá»›i háº¡n MP cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseCap := 1000.0
    
    // Dantian capacity directly affects MP cap (ä¸¹ç”°å®¹é‡ç›´æ¥å½±å“æ³•åŠ›ä¸Šé™) - Dung lÆ°á»£ng Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng trá»±c tiáº¿p giá»›i háº¡n MP
    capacityFactor := dantian.Storage.DantianCapacity / 100.0 * 0.7
    
    // Dantian quality affects MP quality (ä¸¹ç”°è´¨é‡å½±å“æ³•åŠ›è´¨é‡) - Cháº¥t lÆ°á»£ng Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng cháº¥t lÆ°á»£ng MP
    qualityFactor := (dantian.Quality.DantianPurity + dantian.Quality.DantianEfficiency) / 2.0 * 150.0 * 0.2
    
    // Meridian capacity affects qi storage (ç»è„‰å®¹é‡å½±å“æ°”å­˜å‚¨) - Dung lÆ°á»£ng kinh máº¡ch áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng lÆ°u trá»¯ khÃ­
    meridianFactor := meridians.MeridianCapacity.TotalCapacity / 10000.0 * 0.1
    
    return baseCap + capacityFactor + qualityFactor + meridianFactor
}

// Calculate MP consumption efficiency from dantian (ä»ä¸¹ç”°è®¡ç®—æ³•åŠ›æ¶ˆè€—æ•ˆç‡) - TÃ­nh hiá»‡u suáº¥t tiÃªu hao MP tá»« Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
func CalculateMPConsumptionEfficiency(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem) float64 {
    // Base efficiency (åŸºç¡€æ•ˆç‡) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseEfficiency := 1.0
    
    // Dantian efficiency affects MP usage (ä¸¹ç”°æ•ˆç‡å½±å“æ³•åŠ›ä½¿ç”¨) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng sá»­ dá»¥ng MP
    efficiencyFactor := dantian.Quality.DantianEfficiency * 0.4
    
    // Dantian stability affects consistent MP usage (ä¸¹ç”°ç¨³å®šæ€§å½±å“æŒç»­æ³•åŠ›ä½¿ç”¨) - Äá»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng sá»­ dá»¥ng MP liÃªn tá»¥c
    stabilityFactor := dantian.Quality.DantianStability * 0.3
    
    // Meridian efficiency affects qi flow (ç»è„‰æ•ˆç‡å½±å“æ°”æµåŠ¨) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t kinh máº¡ch áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng dÃ²ng cháº£y khÃ­
    meridianFactor := (meridians.MeridianQuality.Conductivity + meridians.MeridianQuality.Toughness) / 2.0 * 0.3
    
    return baseEfficiency + efficiencyFactor + stabilityFactor + meridianFactor
}
```

#### **3. Derived Stats tá»« Äan Äiá»n cho HP/MP**
```go
// Dantian-derived HP/MP stats (ä¸¹ç”°æ´¾ç”Ÿç”Ÿå‘½/æ³•åŠ›å±æ€§) - CÃ¡c derived stats HP/MP tá»« Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
var DantianHPMPStats = []string{
    // HP-related stats (ç”Ÿå‘½ç›¸å…³å±æ€§) - Stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n HP
    "hp_max",                    // Maximum HP (æœ€å¤§ç”Ÿå‘½å€¼) - HP tá»‘i Ä‘a
    "hp_current",                // Current HP (å½“å‰ç”Ÿå‘½å€¼) - HP hiá»‡n táº¡i
    "hp_regeneration",           // HP regeneration rate (ç”Ÿå‘½æ¢å¤ç‡) - Tá»· lá»‡ há»“i phá»¥c HP
    "hp_cap",                    // HP cap (ç”Ÿå‘½ä¸Šé™) - Giá»›i háº¡n HP
    "life_force",                // Life force (ç”Ÿå‘½åŠ›) - Sinh lá»±c
    "vitality",                  // Vitality (æ´»åŠ›) - Sá»©c sá»‘ng
    
    // MP-related stats (æ³•åŠ›ç›¸å…³å±æ€§) - Stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n MP
    "mp_max",                    // Maximum MP (æœ€å¤§æ³•åŠ›å€¼) - MP tá»‘i Ä‘a
    "mp_current",                // Current MP (å½“å‰æ³•åŠ›å€¼) - MP hiá»‡n táº¡i
    "mp_regeneration",           // MP regeneration rate (æ³•åŠ›æ¢å¤ç‡) - Tá»· lá»‡ há»“i phá»¥c MP
    "mp_cap",                    // MP cap (æ³•åŠ›ä¸Šé™) - Giá»›i háº¡n MP
    "qi_reserve",                // Qi reserve (æ°”å‚¨å¤‡) - Dá»± trá»¯ khÃ­
    "spiritual_energy",          // Spiritual energy (ç²¾ç¥èƒ½é‡) - NÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng tinh tháº§n
    "mp_consumption_efficiency", // MP consumption efficiency (æ³•åŠ›æ¶ˆè€—æ•ˆç‡) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t tiÃªu hao MP
    "qi_quality",                // Qi quality (æ°”è´¨é‡) - Cháº¥t lÆ°á»£ng khÃ­
}

// Calculate dantian-derived HP/MP stats (è®¡ç®—ä¸¹ç”°æ´¾ç”Ÿç”Ÿå‘½/æ³•åŠ›å±æ€§) - TÃ­nh cÃ¡c derived stats HP/MP tá»« Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
func CalculateDantianHPMPStats(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem) map[string]float64 {
    stats := make(map[string]float64)
    
    // HP-related stats (ç”Ÿå‘½ç›¸å…³å±æ€§) - Stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n HP
    stats["hp_max"] = CalculateHPFromDantian(dantian, meridians)
    stats["hp_current"] = stats["hp_max"] // Start at full HP
    stats["hp_regeneration"] = CalculateHPRegeneration(dantian, meridians)
    stats["hp_cap"] = CalculateHPCap(dantian, meridians)
    stats["life_force"] = dantian.Storage.DantianCapacity / 1000.0 * 0.8 + dantian.Quality.DantianPurity * 0.2
    stats["vitality"] = dantian.Quality.DantianEfficiency * 0.6 + dantian.Quality.DantianStability * 0.4
    
    // MP-related stats (æ³•åŠ›ç›¸å…³å±æ€§) - Stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n MP
    stats["mp_max"] = CalculateMPFromDantian(dantian, meridians)
    stats["mp_current"] = stats["mp_max"] // Start at full MP
    stats["mp_regeneration"] = CalculateMPRegeneration(dantian, meridians)
    stats["mp_cap"] = CalculateMPCap(dantian, meridians)
    stats["qi_reserve"] = dantian.Storage.DantianCapacity / 1000.0 * 0.9 + dantian.Quality.DantianPurity * 0.1
    stats["spiritual_energy"] = dantian.Quality.DantianPurity * 0.7 + dantian.Quality.DantianEfficiency * 0.3
    stats["mp_consumption_efficiency"] = CalculateMPConsumptionEfficiency(dantian, meridians)
    stats["qi_quality"] = dantian.Quality.DantianPurity * 0.8 + dantian.Quality.DantianEfficiency * 0.2
    
    return stats
}
```

#### **4. áº¢nh HÆ°á»Ÿng Äáº¿n Combat vÃ  Cultivation**

**Combat System:**
```go
// Calculate damage taken with HP (è®¡ç®—å—ä¼¤å®³) - TÃ­nh sÃ¡t thÆ°Æ¡ng nháº­n vÃ o
func CalculateDamageTaken(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem, incomingDamage float64) float64 {
    // Dantian stability reduces damage (ä¸¹ç”°ç¨³å®šæ€§å‡å°‘ä¼¤å®³) - Äá»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n giáº£m sÃ¡t thÆ°Æ¡ng
    stabilityReduction := dantian.Quality.DantianStability * 0.1
    
    // Meridian health provides damage resistance (ç»è„‰å¥åº·æä¾›ä¼¤å®³æŠ—æ€§) - Sá»©c khá»e kinh máº¡ch cung cáº¥p khÃ¡ng sÃ¡t thÆ°Æ¡ng
    meridianResistance := CalculateMainChannelHealth(meridians.MeridianChannels.MainChannels) * 0.05
    
    totalReduction := stabilityReduction + meridianResistance
    if totalReduction > 0.5 {
        totalReduction = 0.5 // Cap at 50% reduction
    }
    
    return incomingDamage * (1.0 - totalReduction)
}

// Calculate spell cost with MP efficiency (è®¡ç®—æ³•æœ¯æ¶ˆè€—) - TÃ­nh chi phÃ­ phÃ¡p thuáº­t
func CalculateSpellCost(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem, baseCost float64) float64 {
    // MP consumption efficiency reduces spell cost (æ³•åŠ›æ¶ˆè€—æ•ˆç‡å‡å°‘æ³•æœ¯æ¶ˆè€—) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t tiÃªu hao MP giáº£m chi phÃ­ phÃ¡p thuáº­t
    efficiency := CalculateMPConsumptionEfficiency(dantian, meridians)
    
    return baseCost / efficiency
}
```

**Cultivation System:**
```go
// Calculate cultivation efficiency with HP/MP (è®¡ç®—ä¿®ç‚¼æ•ˆç‡) - TÃ­nh hiá»‡u suáº¥t tu luyá»‡n
func CalculateCultivationEfficiency(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem) float64 {
    // Base efficiency (åŸºç¡€æ•ˆç‡) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseEfficiency := 1.0
    
    // HP affects cultivation stability (ç”Ÿå‘½å€¼å½±å“ä¿®ç‚¼ç¨³å®šæ€§) - HP áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng Ä‘á»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh tu luyá»‡n
    hpFactor := CalculateHPFromDantian(dantian, meridians) / 1000.0 * 0.3
    
    // MP affects cultivation power (æ³•åŠ›å€¼å½±å“ä¿®ç‚¼åŠ›é‡) - MP áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng sá»©c máº¡nh tu luyá»‡n
    mpFactor := CalculateMPFromDantian(dantian, meridians) / 1000.0 * 0.4
    
    // Dantian quality affects overall efficiency (ä¸¹ç”°è´¨é‡å½±å“æ•´ä½“æ•ˆç‡) - Cháº¥t lÆ°á»£ng Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng hiá»‡u suáº¥t tá»•ng thá»ƒ
    qualityFactor := (dantian.Quality.DantianPurity + dantian.Quality.DantianEfficiency) / 2.0 * 0.3
    
    return baseEfficiency + hpFactor + mpFactor + qualityFactor
}
```

### **3. Thá»©c Háº£i (Spirit Sea) - Trung TÃ¢m Tháº§n Thá»©c**

#### **Äá»‹nh NghÄ©a Thá»©c Háº£i vÃ  Tháº§n Thá»©c**

**Thá»©c Háº£i (Spirit Sea)** lÃ  trung tÃ¢m cá»§a tháº§n thá»©c, tÆ°Æ¡ng tá»± nhÆ° "consciousness" trong tÃ¢m lÃ½ há»c hiá»‡n Ä‘áº¡i. ÄÃ¢y lÃ  nÆ¡i chá»©a Ä‘á»±ng:

1. **Tháº§n Thá»©c (Divine Consciousness)** - Kháº£ nÄƒng nháº­n thá»©c vÃ  Ä‘iá»u khiá»ƒn
2. **Niá»‡m Lá»±c (Mental Force)** - NÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng tinh tháº§n Ä‘á»ƒ thá»±c hiá»‡n cÃ¡c hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng tÃ¢m linh
3. **TrÃ­ Tuá»‡ (Wisdom)** - Kháº£ nÄƒng hiá»ƒu biáº¿t vÃ  phÃ¢n tÃ­ch
4. **Ã ChÃ­ (Willpower)** - Sá»©c máº¡nh tinh tháº§n Ä‘á»ƒ vÆ°á»£t qua khÃ³ khÄƒn

**Tháº§n Thá»©c (Divine Consciousness)** trong xianxia cÃ³ vai trÃ² tÆ°Æ¡ng tá»± nhÆ° **Magic/Intelligence** trong RPG:

- **Cao Tháº§n Thá»©c** = **Cao Magic** â†’ Cast spell damage cao hÆ¡n
- **Cao Tháº§n Thá»©c** = **Cao Intelligence** â†’ Hiá»ƒu biáº¿t phÃ¡p thuáº­t tá»‘t hÆ¡n
- **Cao Tháº§n Thá»©c** = **Cao Control** â†’ Äiá»u khiá»ƒn phÃ¡p báº£o, luyá»‡n Ä‘an, bÃ y tráº­n phÃ¡p tá»‘t hÆ¡n

#### **Cáº¥u TrÃºc Thá»©c Háº£i**

```go
    // Basic cultivation mind (åŸºç¡€ä¿®ç‚¼å¿ƒå¢ƒ) - TÃ¢m cáº£nh tu luyá»‡n cÆ¡ báº£n
    Calmness         float64 `json:"calmness"`            // Calmness (å¹³é™) - BÃ¬nh tÄ©nh
    Serenity         float64 `json:"serenity"`            // Serenity (å®é™) - TÄ©nh láº·ng
    Tranquility      float64 `json:"tranquility"`         // Tranquility (å®é™) - An tÄ©nh
    Peace            float64 `json:"peace"`               // Peace (å’Œå¹³) - HÃ²a bÃ¬nh
    Harmony          float64 `json:"harmony"`             // Harmony (å’Œè°) - HÃ i hÃ²a
    
    // Advanced cultivation mind (é«˜çº§ä¿®ç‚¼å¿ƒå¢ƒ) - TÃ¢m cáº£nh tu luyá»‡n nÃ¢ng cao
    Enlightenment    float64 `json:"enlightenment"`       // Enlightenment (å¼€æ‚Ÿ) - Khai ngá»™
    Transcendence    float64 `json:"transcendence"`       // Transcendence (è¶…è„±) - SiÃªu thoÃ¡t
    Nirvana          float64 `json:"nirvana"`             // Nirvana (æ¶…æ§ƒ) - Niáº¿t bÃ n
    Buddhahood       float64 `json:"buddhahood"`          // Buddhahood (ä½›æ€§) - Pháº­t tÃ­nh
    DaoHeart         float64 `json:"dao_heart"`           // Dao Heart (é“å¿ƒ) - Äáº¡o tÃ¢m
}
```

```go
// Calculate Spirit Sea primary stats (è®¡ç®—è¯†æµ·ä¸»è¦å±æ€§) - TÃ­nh cÃ¡c primary stats tá»« thá»©c háº£i
func CalculateSpiritSeaPrimaryStats(spiritSea SpiritSeaSystem) map[string]float64 {
    stats := make(map[string]float64)
    
    // Core stats (æ ¸å¿ƒå±æ€§) - Thuá»™c tÃ­nh cá»‘t lÃµi
    stats["shen_clarity"] = spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenClarity
    stats["shen_control"] = spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenControl
    stats["shen_capacity"] = spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenCapacity
    stats["shen_stability"] = spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenStability
    stats["shen_efficiency"] = spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenEfficiency
    
    // Advanced stats (é«˜çº§å±æ€§) - Thuá»™c tÃ­nh nÃ¢ng cao
    stats["divine_awareness"] = spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.DivineAwareness
    stats["spiritual_range"] = spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.SpiritualRange
    stats["mental_resistance"] = spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.MentalResistance
    stats["thought_speed"] = spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ThoughtSpeed
    stats["memory_capacity"] = spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.MemoryCapacity
    
    // Consciousness stats (æ„è¯†å±æ€§) - Thuá»™c tÃ­nh Ã½ thá»©c
    stats["basic_consciousness"] = spiritSea.Consciousness.BasicConsciousness
    stats["advanced_consciousness"] = spiritSea.Consciousness.AdvancedConsciousness
    stats["divine_consciousness"] = spiritSea.Consciousness.DivineConsciousness
    stats["transcendent_consciousness"] = spiritSea.Consciousness.TranscendentConsciousness
    
    // Mental force stats (å¿µåŠ›å±æ€§) - Thuá»™c tÃ­nh niá»‡m lá»±c
    stats["nian_li_capacity"] = spiritSea.MentalForce.NianLiCapacity
    stats["nian_li_current"] = spiritSea.MentalForce.NianLiCurrent
    stats["nian_li_regen"] = spiritSea.MentalForce.NianLiRegen
    stats["nian_li_efficiency"] = spiritSea.MentalForce.NianLiEfficiency
    
    // Wisdom stats (æ™ºæ…§å±æ€§) - Thuá»™c tÃ­nh trÃ­ tuá»‡
    stats["knowledge"] = spiritSea.Wisdom.Knowledge
    stats["understanding"] = spiritSea.Wisdom.Understanding
    stats["analysis"] = spiritSea.Wisdom.Analysis
    stats["synthesis"] = spiritSea.Wisdom.Synthesis
    stats["intuition"] = spiritSea.Wisdom.Intuition
    
    // Willpower stats (æ„å¿—åŠ›å±æ€§) - Thuá»™c tÃ­nh Ã½ chÃ­
    stats["determination"] = spiritSea.Willpower.Determination
    stats["perseverance"] = spiritSea.Willpower.Perseverance
    stats["resilience"] = spiritSea.Willpower.Resilience
    stats["courage"] = spiritSea.Willpower.Courage
    stats["discipline"] = spiritSea.Willpower.Discipline
    
    // Divine sense stats (ç¥å¿µå±æ€§) - Thuá»™c tÃ­nh tháº§n niá»‡m
    stats["sense_range"] = spiritSea.DivineSense.SenseRange
    stats["sense_precision"] = spiritSea.DivineSense.SensePrecision
    stats["sense_speed"] = spiritSea.DivineSense.SenseSpeed
    stats["sense_penetration"] = spiritSea.DivineSense.SensePenetration
    stats["sense_stealth"] = spiritSea.DivineSense.SenseStealth
    
    // Spiritual control stats (ç²¾ç¥æ§åˆ¶å±æ€§) - Thuá»™c tÃ­nh Ä‘iá»u khiá»ƒn tinh tháº§n
    stats["self_control"] = spiritSea.SpiritualControl.SelfControl
    stats["emotion_control"] = spiritSea.SpiritualControl.EmotionControl
    stats["thought_control"] = spiritSea.SpiritualControl.ThoughtControl
    stats["memory_control"] = spiritSea.SpiritualControl.MemoryControl
    stats["dream_control"] = spiritSea.SpiritualControl.DreamControl
    
    // Memory palace stats (è®°å¿†å®«æ®¿å±æ€§) - Thuá»™c tÃ­nh cung Ä‘iá»‡n kÃ½ á»©c
    stats["memory_speed"] = spiritSea.MemoryPalace.MemorySpeed
    stats["memory_accuracy"] = spiritSea.MemoryPalace.MemoryAccuracy
    stats["memory_retention"] = spiritSea.MemoryPalace.MemoryRetention
    stats["memory_recall"] = spiritSea.MemoryPalace.MemoryRecall
    
    // Cultivation mind stats (ä¿®ç‚¼å¿ƒå¢ƒå±æ€§) - Thuá»™c tÃ­nh tÃ¢m cáº£nh tu luyá»‡n
    stats["calmness"] = spiritSea.CultivationMind.Calmness
    stats["serenity"] = spiritSea.CultivationMind.Serenity
    stats["tranquility"] = spiritSea.CultivationMind.Tranquility
    stats["peace"] = spiritSea.CultivationMind.Peace
    stats["harmony"] = spiritSea.CultivationMind.Harmony
    
    return stats
}
```

#### **TÃ­nh Niá»‡m Lá»±c tá»« Thá»©c Háº£i**
```go
// Calculate Nian Li from Spirit Sea (ä»è¯†æµ·è®¡ç®—å¿µåŠ›) - TÃ­nh niá»‡m lá»±c tá»« thá»©c háº£i
func CalculateNianLiFromSpiritSea(spiritSea SpiritSeaSystem) float64 {
    // Base Nian Li (åŸºç¡€å¿µåŠ›) - Niá»‡m lá»±c cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseNianLi := 0.0
    
    // Shen capacity affects Nian Li capacity (ç¥å®¹å½±å“å¿µåŠ›å®¹é‡) - Tháº§n dung áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng dung lÆ°á»£ng niá»‡m lá»±c
    shenCapacityFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenCapacity / 1000.0 * 0.4
    
    // Shen control affects Nian Li control (ç¥æ§å½±å“å¿µåŠ›æ§åˆ¶) - Tháº§n khá»‘ng áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng Ä‘iá»u khiá»ƒn niá»‡m lá»±c
    shenControlFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenControl * 0.3
    
    // Shen clarity affects Nian Li precision (ç¥æ¸…å½±å“å¿µåŠ›ç²¾åº¦) - Tháº§n thanh áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng Ä‘á»™ chÃ­nh xÃ¡c niá»‡m lá»±c
    shenClarityFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenClarity * 0.2
    
    // Shen efficiency affects Nian Li efficiency (ç¥æ•ˆå½±å“å¿µåŠ›æ•ˆç‡) - Tháº§n hiá»‡u áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng hiá»‡u suáº¥t niá»‡m lá»±c
    shenEfficiencyFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenEfficiency * 0.1
    
    return baseNianLi + shenCapacityFactor + shenControlFactor + shenClarityFactor + shenEfficiencyFactor
}

// Calculate Nian Li regeneration from Spirit Sea (ä»è¯†æµ·è®¡ç®—å¿µåŠ›æ¢å¤) - TÃ­nh há»“i phá»¥c niá»‡m lá»±c tá»« thá»©c háº£i
func CalculateNianLiRegeneration(spiritSea SpiritSeaSystem) float64 {
    // Base regen rate (åŸºç¡€æ¢å¤ç‡) - Tá»· lá»‡ há»“i phá»¥c cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseRegen := 0.1
    
    // Shen efficiency affects Nian Li regen (ç¥æ•ˆå½±å“å¿µåŠ›æ¢å¤) - Tháº§n hiá»‡u áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng há»“i phá»¥c niá»‡m lá»±c
    efficiencyFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenEfficiency * 0.5
    
    // Shen stability affects consistent regen (ç¥ç¨³å½±å“æŒç»­æ¢å¤) - Tháº§n á»•n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng há»“i phá»¥c liÃªn tá»¥c
    stabilityFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenStability * 0.3
    
    // Consciousness level affects regen speed (æ„è¯†å±‚æ¬¡å½±å“æ¢å¤é€Ÿåº¦) - Má»©c Ä‘á»™ Ã½ thá»©c áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ há»“i phá»¥c
    consciousnessFactor := (spiritSea.Consciousness.BasicConsciousness + 
                           spiritSea.Consciousness.AdvancedConsciousness + 
                           spiritSea.Consciousness.DivineConsciousness) / 3.0 * 0.2
    
    return baseRegen + efficiencyFactor + stabilityFactor + consciousnessFactor
}

// Calculate Nian Li cap from Spirit Sea (ä»è¯†æµ·è®¡ç®—å¿µåŠ›ä¸Šé™) - TÃ­nh giá»›i háº¡n niá»‡m lá»±c tá»« thá»©c háº£i
func CalculateNianLiCap(spiritSea SpiritSeaSystem) float64 {
    // Base cap (åŸºç¡€ä¸Šé™) - Giá»›i háº¡n cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseCap := 50000.0
    
    // Shen capacity directly affects Nian Li cap (ç¥å®¹ç›´æ¥å½±å“å¿µåŠ›ä¸Šé™) - Tháº§n dung áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng trá»±c tiáº¿p giá»›i háº¡n niá»‡m lá»±c
    capacityFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenCapacity / 100.0 * 0.6
    
    // Shen clarity affects Nian Li quality (ç¥æ¸…å½±å“å¿µåŠ›è´¨é‡) - Tháº§n thanh áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng cháº¥t lÆ°á»£ng niá»‡m lá»±c
    clarityFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenClarity * 100.0 * 0.3
    
    // Divine consciousness affects Nian Li power (ç¥æ„è¯†å½±å“å¿µåŠ›åŠ›é‡) - Tháº§n Ã½ thá»©c áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng sá»©c máº¡nh niá»‡m lá»±c
    consciousnessFactor := spiritSea.Consciousness.DivineConsciousness * 50.0 * 0.1
    
    return baseCap + capacityFactor + clarityFactor + consciousnessFactor
}
```

#### **áº¢nh HÆ°á»Ÿng cá»§a Tháº§n Thá»©c Ä‘áº¿n Combat**
```go
// Calculate spell damage from Shen (ä»ç¥è®¡ç®—æ³•æœ¯ä¼¤å®³) - TÃ­nh sÃ¡t thÆ°Æ¡ng phÃ¡p thuáº­t tá»« tháº§n
func CalculateSpellDamageFromShen(spiritSea SpiritSeaSystem, baseDamage float64) float64 {
    // Base damage (åŸºç¡€ä¼¤å®³) - SÃ¡t thÆ°Æ¡ng cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseSpellDamage := baseDamage
    
    // Shen control affects spell power (ç¥æ§å½±å“æ³•æœ¯å¨åŠ›) - Tháº§n khá»‘ng áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng uy lá»±c phÃ¡p thuáº­t
    shenControlFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenControl * 0.4
    
    // Shen clarity affects spell precision (ç¥æ¸…å½±å“æ³•æœ¯ç²¾åº¦) - Tháº§n thanh áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng Ä‘á»™ chÃ­nh xÃ¡c phÃ¡p thuáº­t
    shenClarityFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenClarity * 0.3
    
    // Shen efficiency affects spell efficiency (ç¥æ•ˆå½±å“æ³•æœ¯æ•ˆç‡) - Tháº§n hiá»‡u áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng hiá»‡u suáº¥t phÃ¡p thuáº­t
    shenEfficiencyFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenEfficiency * 0.2
    
    // Divine consciousness affects spell power (ç¥æ„è¯†å½±å“æ³•æœ¯å¨åŠ›) - Tháº§n Ã½ thá»©c áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng uy lá»±c phÃ¡p thuáº­t
    consciousnessFactor := spiritSea.Consciousness.DivineConsciousness * 0.1
    
    return baseSpellDamage * (1.0 + shenControlFactor + shenClarityFactor + shenEfficiencyFactor + consciousnessFactor)
}

// Calculate spell accuracy from Shen (ä»ç¥è®¡ç®—æ³•æœ¯å‘½ä¸­) - TÃ­nh Ä‘á»™ chÃ­nh xÃ¡c phÃ¡p thuáº­t tá»« tháº§n
func CalculateSpellAccuracyFromShen(spiritSea SpiritSeaSystem) float64 {
    // Base accuracy (åŸºç¡€å‘½ä¸­) - Äá»™ chÃ­nh xÃ¡c cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseAccuracy := 0.8
    
    // Shen clarity affects accuracy (ç¥æ¸…å½±å“å‘½ä¸­) - Tháº§n thanh áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng Ä‘á»™ chÃ­nh xÃ¡c
    clarityFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenClarity * 0.3
    
    // Shen control affects control (ç¥æ§å½±å“æ§åˆ¶) - Tháº§n khá»‘ng áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng Ä‘iá»u khiá»ƒn
    controlFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenControl * 0.2
    
    // Divine sense affects precision (ç¥å¿µå½±å“ç²¾åº¦) - Tháº§n niá»‡m áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng Ä‘á»™ chÃ­nh xÃ¡c
    senseFactor := spiritSea.DivineSense.SensePrecision * 0.1
    
    return baseAccuracy + clarityFactor + controlFactor + senseFactor
}

// Calculate spell range from Shen (ä»ç¥è®¡ç®—æ³•æœ¯èŒƒå›´) - TÃ­nh pháº¡m vi phÃ¡p thuáº­t tá»« tháº§n
func CalculateSpellRangeFromShen(spiritSea SpiritSeaSystem) float64 {
    // Base range (åŸºç¡€èŒƒå›´) - Pháº¡m vi cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseRange := 10.0
    
    // Spiritual range affects spell range (ç¥åŸŸå½±å“æ³•æœ¯èŒƒå›´) - Tháº§n vá»±c áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng pháº¡m vi phÃ¡p thuáº­t
    rangeFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.SpiritualRange * 0.5
    
    // Divine sense affects range (ç¥å¿µå½±å“èŒƒå›´) - Tháº§n niá»‡m áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng pháº¡m vi
    senseFactor := spiritSea.DivineSense.SenseRange * 0.3
    
    // Advanced consciousness affects range (é«˜çº§æ„è¯†å½±å“èŒƒå›´) - Ã thá»©c nÃ¢ng cao áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng pháº¡m vi
    consciousnessFactor := spiritSea.Consciousness.AdvancedConsciousness * 0.2
    
    return baseRange + rangeFactor + senseFactor + consciousnessFactor
}

// Calculate spell cooldown from Shen (ä»ç¥è®¡ç®—æ³•æœ¯å†·å´) - TÃ­nh thá»i gian há»“i chiÃªu phÃ¡p thuáº­t tá»« tháº§n
func CalculateSpellCooldownFromShen(spiritSea SpiritSeaSystem, baseCooldown float64) float64 {
    // Base cooldown (åŸºç¡€å†·å´) - Thá»i gian há»“i chiÃªu cÆ¡ báº£n
    baseSpellCooldown := baseCooldown
    
    // Shen efficiency affects cooldown (ç¥æ•ˆå½±å“å†·å´) - Tháº§n hiá»‡u áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng thá»i gian há»“i chiÃªu
    efficiencyFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenEfficiency * 0.3
    
    // Shen stability affects consistency (ç¥ç¨³å½±å“ä¸€è‡´æ€§) - Tháº§n á»•n áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng tÃ­nh nháº¥t quÃ¡n
    stabilityFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenStability * 0.2
    
    // Thought speed affects casting speed (ç¥é€Ÿå½±å“æ–½æ³•é€Ÿåº¦) - Tháº§n tá»‘c áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ thi triá»ƒn
    speedFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ThoughtSpeed * 0.1
    
    return baseSpellCooldown / (1.0 + efficiencyFactor + stabilityFactor + speedFactor)
}
```

### **3. Thá»©c Háº£i (Spirit Sea) - Trung TÃ¢m Tháº§n Thá»©c**
Thá»©c háº£i lÃ  trung tÃ¢m cá»§a tháº§n thá»©c, áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng Ä‘áº¿n cÃ¡c primary stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n **Tháº§n** vÃ  **Ä‘iá»u khiá»ƒn**:

#### **Primary Stats tá»« Thá»©c Háº£i:**
```go
// Spirit Sea-related primary stats (è¯†æµ·ç›¸å…³ä¸»è¦å±æ€§) - CÃ¡c primary stats tá»« thá»©c háº£i
var SpiritSeaPrimaryStats = []string{
    "shen_depth",           // Shen depth (ç¥æ·±åº¦) - Äá»™ sÃ¢u thá»©c háº£i
    "shen_clarity",         // Shen clarity (ç¥æ¸…æ™°åº¦) - Äá»™ tinh tÆ°á»ng cá»§a Tháº§n
    "shen_control",         // Shen control (ç¥æ§åˆ¶) - NÄƒng lá»±c Ä‘iá»u khiá»ƒn
    "spirit_sea_capacity",  // Spirit sea capacity (è¯†æµ·å®¹é‡) - Dung lÆ°á»£ng thá»©c háº£i
    "spirit_sea_stability", // Spirit sea stability (è¯†æµ·ç¨³å®šæ€§) - Äá»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh thá»©c háº£i
    "dao_comprehension",    // Dao comprehension (é“ç†è§£) - Ngá»™ tÃ­nh/Ä‘áº¡o háº¡nh
}
```

#### **Cáº¥u TrÃºc Thá»©c Háº£i:**
```go
type SpiritSea struct {
    // Spirit sea core (è¯†æµ·æ ¸å¿ƒ) - LÃµi thá»©c háº£i
    SpiritSeaCore SpiritSeaCore `json:"spirit_sea_core"`
    
    // Spirit sea capacity (è¯†æµ·å®¹é‡) - Dung lÆ°á»£ng thá»©c háº£i
    SpiritSeaCapacity SpiritSeaCapacity `json:"spirit_sea_capacity"`
    
    // Dao comprehension (é“ç†è§£) - Ngá»™ tÃ­nh Ä‘áº¡o
    DaoComprehension DaoComprehension `json:"dao_comprehension"`
}

type SpiritSeaCore struct {
    ShenDepth        float64 `json:"shen_depth"`        // 0.0 - 1.0 (ç¥æ·±åº¦) - Äá»™ sÃ¢u thá»©c háº£i
    ShenClarity      float64 `json:"shen_clarity"`      // 0.0 - 1.0 (ç¥æ¸…æ™°åº¦) - Äá»™ tinh tÆ°á»ng
    ShenControl      float64 `json:"shen_control"`      // 0.0 - 1.0 (ç¥æ§åˆ¶) - NÄƒng lá»±c Ä‘iá»u khiá»ƒn
    OverallShen      float64 `json:"overall_shen"`      // Average of above (æ•´ä½“ç¥) - Tháº§n tá»•ng há»£p
}

type SpiritSeaCapacity struct {
    MaxSpiritPower   float64 `json:"max_spirit_power"`  // Maximum spirit power (æœ€å¤§ç¥è¯†åŠ›) - Tháº§n thá»©c lá»±c tá»‘i Ä‘a
    CurrentSpiritPower float64 `json:"current_spirit_power"` // Current spirit power (å½“å‰ç¥è¯†åŠ›) - Tháº§n thá»©c lá»±c hiá»‡n táº¡i
    SpiritRegeneration float64 `json:"spirit_regeneration"` // Spirit regeneration rate (ç¥è¯†æ¢å¤é€Ÿç‡) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ há»“i tháº§n
    TotalCapacity    float64 `json:"total_capacity"`    // Total spirit sea capacity (æ€»è¯†æµ·å®¹é‡) - Tá»•ng dung lÆ°á»£ng thá»©c háº£i
}

type DaoComprehension struct {
    DaoLevel         float64 `json:"dao_level"`         // 0.0 - 1.0 (é“ç­‰çº§) - Cáº¥p Ä‘á»™ Ä‘áº¡o
    ComprehensionRate float64 `json:"comprehension_rate"` // 0.0 - 1.0 (ç†è§£é€Ÿç‡) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ lÄ©nh ngá»™
    DaoAffinity      float64 `json:"dao_affinity"`      // 0.0 - 1.0 (é“äº²å’ŒåŠ›) - Äá»™ tÆ°Æ¡ng thÃ­ch vá»›i Ä‘áº¡o
}
```

#### **CÃ´ng Thá»©c TÃ­nh ToÃ¡n Thá»©c Háº£i:**
```go
// Calculate spirit sea-related stats (è®¡ç®—è¯†æµ·ç›¸å…³å±æ€§) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n cÃ¡c stats liÃªn quan Ä‘áº¿n thá»©c háº£i
func CalculateSpiritSeaStats(spiritSea SpiritSea) map[string]float64 {
    stats := make(map[string]float64)
    
    // Shen depth (ç¥æ·±åº¦) - Äá»™ sÃ¢u thá»©c háº£i
    stats["shen_depth"] = spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenDepth
    
    // Shen clarity (ç¥æ¸…æ™°åº¦) - Äá»™ tinh tÆ°á»ng cá»§a Tháº§n
    stats["shen_clarity"] = spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenClarity
    
    // Shen control (ç¥æ§åˆ¶) - NÄƒng lá»±c Ä‘iá»u khiá»ƒn
    stats["shen_control"] = spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenControl
    
    // Spirit sea capacity (è¯†æµ·å®¹é‡) - Dung lÆ°á»£ng thá»©c háº£i
    stats["spirit_sea_capacity"] = spiritSea.SpiritSeaCapacity.TotalCapacity
    
    // Spirit sea stability (è¯†æµ·ç¨³å®šæ€§) - Äá»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh thá»©c háº£i = (ShenDepth + ShenClarity) / 2
    stats["spirit_sea_stability"] = (spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenDepth + spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenClarity) / 2.0
    
    // Dao comprehension (é“ç†è§£) - Ngá»™ tÃ­nh Ä‘áº¡o
    stats["dao_comprehension"] = spiritSea.DaoComprehension.DaoLevel
    
    return stats
}
```

### **TÃ³m Táº¯t Há»‡ Thá»‘ng 3 ThÃ nh Pháº§n**

#### **Báº£ng PhÃ¢n Chia Primary Stats:**
| ThÃ nh Pháº§n | Primary Stats | Chá»©c NÄƒng ChÃ­nh | áº¢nh HÆ°á»Ÿng Äáº¿n |
|------------|---------------|------------------|---------------|
| **Äan Äiá»n** | `dantian_capacity`, `dantian_compression`, `dantian_stability`, `dantian_purity`, `qi_purity`, `eff_jing_to_qi`, `eff_qi_to_shen`, `cultivation_exp` | LÆ°u trá»¯ vÃ  chuyá»ƒn hÃ³a khÃ­ | Tu luyá»‡n, breakthrough, chuyá»ƒn hÃ³a nÄƒng lÆ°á»£ng |
| **Kinh Máº¡ch** | `meridian_conductivity`, `meridian_toughness`, `meridian_purity_resistance`, `jing_reserve`, `meridian_efficiency`, `meridian_capacity` | Váº­n chuyá»ƒn khÃ­ trong cÆ¡ thá»ƒ | Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ tu luyá»‡n, kháº£ nÄƒng chá»‹u Ã¡p lá»±c, lÆ°u thÃ´ng khÃ­ |
| **Thá»©c Háº£i** | `shen_depth`, `shen_clarity`, `shen_control`, `spirit_sea_capacity`, `spirit_sea_stability`, `dao_comprehension` | Äiá»u khiá»ƒn tháº§n thá»©c | Äiá»u khiá»ƒn phÃ¡p báº£o, luyá»‡n kim, bÃ y tráº­n phÃ¡p, lÄ©nh ngá»™ Ä‘áº¡o |

#### **VÃ­ Dá»¥ áº¢nh HÆ°á»Ÿng Äáº¿n CÃ¡c Hoáº¡t Äá»™ng:**

**1. Äiá»u Khiá»ƒn PhÃ¡p Báº£o (Artifact Control):**
```go
// Artifact control effectiveness (æ³•å®æ§åˆ¶æ•ˆæœ) - Hiá»‡u quáº£ Ä‘iá»u khiá»ƒn phÃ¡p báº£o
func CalculateArtifactControlEffectiveness(spiritSea SpiritSea) float64 {
    // Dá»±a trÃªn shen_control vÃ  shen_clarity
    return spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenControl * 0.7 + spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenClarity * 0.3
}
```

**2. Luyá»‡n Kim (Alchemy):**
```go
// Alchemy success rate (ç‚¼ä¸¹æˆåŠŸç‡) - Tá»· lá»‡ thÃ nh cÃ´ng luyá»‡n kim
func CalculateAlchemySuccessRate(dantian DantianInfo, spiritSea SpiritSea) float64 {
    // Dá»±a trÃªn dantian_purity, shen_control, vÃ  dao_comprehension
    dantianFactor := dantian.Quality.DantianPurity * 0.4
    spiritFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenControl * 0.3
    daoFactor := spiritSea.DaoComprehension.DaoLevel * 0.3
    
    return dantianFactor + spiritFactor + daoFactor
}
```

**3. Luyá»‡n KhÃ­ (Qi Refining):**
```go
// Qi refining efficiency (ç‚¼æ°”æ•ˆç‡) - Hiá»‡u suáº¥t luyá»‡n khÃ­
func CalculateQiRefiningEfficiency(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem) float64 {
    // Dá»±a trÃªn dantian_compression, meridian_conductivity, vÃ  qi_purity
    dantianFactor := dantian.Quality.DantianPurity * 0.4
    meridianFactor := meridians.MeridianQuality.Conductivity * 0.4
    compressionFactor := (dantian.Core.TotalCultivationExp / dantian.Storage.DantianCapacity) * 0.2
    
    return dantianFactor + meridianFactor + compressionFactor
}
```

**4. BÃ y Tráº­n PhÃ¡p (Formation Array):**
```go
// Formation array effectiveness (é˜µæ³•æ•ˆæœ) - Hiá»‡u quáº£ bÃ y tráº­n phÃ¡p
func CalculateFormationArrayEffectiveness(spiritSea SpiritSea, meridians MeridianSystem) float64 {
    // Dá»±a trÃªn shen_depth, shen_control, vÃ  meridian_efficiency
    shenFactor := (spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenDepth + spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenControl) / 2.0 * 0.6
    meridianFactor := meridians.MeridianQuality.Conductivity * 0.4
    
    return shenFactor + meridianFactor
}
```

**5. Breakthrough (Äá»™t PhÃ¡):**
```go
// Breakthrough success rate (çªç ´æˆåŠŸç‡) - Tá»· lá»‡ thÃ nh cÃ´ng Ä‘á»™t phÃ¡
func CalculateBreakthroughSuccessRate(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem, spiritSea SpiritSea) float64 {
    // Dá»±a trÃªn táº¥t cáº£ 3 thÃ nh pháº§n
    dantianFactor := dantian.Quality.DantianStability * 0.4
    meridianFactor := meridians.MeridianQuality.Toughness * 0.3
    spiritFactor := spiritSea.SpiritSeaCore.ShenClarity * 0.3
    
    return dantianFactor + meridianFactor + spiritFactor
}
```

### **CÃ´ng Thá»©c Tá»•ng Há»£p Primary Stats:**
```go
// Calculate all primary stats from 3 components (ä»3ä¸ªç»„ä»¶è®¡ç®—æ‰€æœ‰ä¸»è¦å±æ€§) - TÃ­nh toÃ¡n táº¥t cáº£ primary stats tá»« 3 thÃ nh pháº§n
func CalculateAllPrimaryStats(dantian DantianInfo, meridians MeridianSystem, spiritSea SpiritSea) map[string]float64 {
    allStats := make(map[string]float64)
    
    // Merge stats from all 3 components (åˆå¹¶3ä¸ªç»„ä»¶çš„å±æ€§) - Gá»™p stats tá»« 3 thÃ nh pháº§n
    dantianStats := CalculateDantianStats(dantian)
    meridianStats := CalculateMeridianStats(meridians)
    spiritSeaStats := CalculateSpiritSeaStats(spiritSea)
    
    // Add dantian stats (æ·»åŠ ä¸¹ç”°å±æ€§) - ThÃªm stats Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
    for key, value := range dantianStats {
        allStats[key] = value
    }
    
    // Add meridian stats (æ·»åŠ ç»è„‰å±æ€§) - ThÃªm stats kinh máº¡ch
    for key, value := range meridianStats {
        allStats[key] = value
    }
    
    // Add spirit sea stats (æ·»åŠ è¯†æµ·å±æ€§) - ThÃªm stats thá»©c háº£i
    for key, value := range spiritSeaStats {
        allStats[key] = value
    }
    
    return allStats
}
```

#### **3. Derived Stats tá»« Äan Äiá»n**
```go
// Derived stats calculated from dantian (ä»ä¸¹ç”°è®¡ç®—çš„æ´¾ç”Ÿå±æ€§) - CÃ¡c derived stats Ä‘Æ°á»£c tÃ­nh tá»« Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n
var DantianDerivedStats = []string{
    "qi_max",             // Maximum qi (æœ€å¤§æ°”åŠ›) - KhÃ­ lá»±c tá»‘i Ä‘a (dá»±a trÃªn tu vi)
    "qi_regeneration",    // Qi regeneration rate (æ°”åŠ›æ¢å¤é€Ÿåº¦) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ há»“i khÃ­ (dá»±a trÃªn cháº¥t lÆ°á»£ng Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n)
    "cultivation_speed",  // Cultivation speed (ä¿®ç‚¼é€Ÿåº¦) - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ tu luyá»‡n (dá»±a trÃªn Ä‘á»™ tinh khiáº¿t)
    "breakthrough_chance", // Breakthrough chance (çªç ´å‡ ç‡) - Tá»· lá»‡ breakthrough (dá»±a trÃªn Ä‘á»™ á»•n Ä‘á»‹nh)
    "power_level",        // Power level (åŠ›é‡ç­‰çº§) - Power level (dá»±a trÃªn tu vi)
}
```

#### **4. Caps tá»« Äan Äiá»n**
```go
// Caps applied based on dantian (åŸºäºä¸¹ç”°åº”ç”¨çš„é™åˆ¶) - CÃ¡c caps Ä‘Æ°á»£c Ã¡p dá»¥ng dá»±a trÃªn Ä‘an Ä‘iá»n

        Scope: "REALM",
        Mode: "CLAMP_MAX",
    },
}
```

### **CÃ´ng Thá»©c TÃ­nh ToÃ¡n Chi Tiáº¿t**

#### **1. Cultivation Experience â†’ Power Level**
```go
// Convert cultivation experience to power level (å°†ä¿®ç‚¼ç»éªŒè½¬æ¢ä¸ºåŠ›é‡ç­‰çº§) - Tu Vi â†’ Power Level
func CultivationExpToPowerLevel(cultivationExp float64) int64 {
    return int64(cultivationExp / 1000.0)
}
```

#### **2. Power Level â†’ Cultivation Experience**
```go
// Convert power level to cultivation experience (å°†åŠ›é‡ç­‰çº§è½¬æ¢ä¸ºä¿®ç‚¼ç»éªŒ) - Power Level â†’ Tu Vi
func PowerLevelToCultivationExp(powerLevel int64) float64 {
    return float64(powerLevel) * 1000.0
}
```

#### **3. Cultivation Experience â†’ Qi Max**
```go
// Convert cultivation experience to maximum qi (å°†ä¿®ç‚¼ç»éªŒè½¬æ¢ä¸ºæœ€å¤§æ°”åŠ›) - Tu Vi â†’ Qi Max
func CultivationExpToQiMax(cultivationExp float64) float64 {
    return cultivationExp * 100.0 // 1 cultivation exp = 100 qi (1ä¿®ç‚¼ç»éªŒ = 100æ°”åŠ›)
}
```

#### **4. Dantian Quality â†’ Cultivation Speed**
```go
// Convert dantian quality to cultivation speed (å°†ä¸¹ç”°è´¨é‡è½¬æ¢ä¸ºä¿®ç‚¼é€Ÿåº¦) - Cháº¥t LÆ°á»£ng Äan Äiá»n â†’ Tá»‘c Äá»™ Tu Luyá»‡n
func DantianQualityToCultivationSpeed(quality float64) float64 {
    return quality * 1.5 // High quality = faster cultivation (é«˜è´¨é‡ = ä¿®ç‚¼æ›´å¿«)
}
```
